4.2 State Management (Riverpod)
dart
// providers/alert_provider.dart
import 'package:riverpod_annotation/riverpod_annotation.dart';
import 'package:freezed_annotation/freezed_annotation.dart';

part 'alert_provider.freezed.dart';
part 'alert_provider.g.dart';

@freezed
class AlertState with _$AlertState {
  const factory AlertState({
    @Default(false) bool isActive,
    @Default(false) bool isTriggering,
    AlertData? currentAlert,
    @Default([]) List<AlertData> alertHistory,
    DateTime? lastGuardianResponse,
    @Default(false) bool isAudioStreaming,
    @Default(false) bool isVideoRecording,
  }) = _AlertState;
}

@riverpod
class AlertNotifier extends _$AlertNotifier {
  @override
  AlertState build() {
    // Load alert history from local storage
    _loadHistory();
    return const AlertState();
  }
  
  Future<void> triggerEmergency() async {
    state = state.copyWith(isTriggering: true);
    
    try {
      // 1. Get location
      final location = await ref.read(locationServiceProvider).getCurrentLocation();
      
      // 2. Create alert
      final alert = AlertData(
        id: _generateAlertId(),
        triggerTime: DateTime.now(),
        guardiansNotified: ref.read(guardianProvider).activeGuardians.length,
        latitude: location.latitude,
        longitude: location.longitude,
      );
      
      // 3. Start audio recording
      await ref.read(audioServiceProvider).startRecording(alert.id);
      
      // 4. Send HTTP alert
      await ref.read(alertRepositoryProvider).sendAlert(alert);
      
      // 5. Send SMS to guardians
      await ref.read(smsServiceProvider).sendEmergencySms(
        ref.read(guardianProvider).activeGuardians,
        alert,
      );
      
      // 6. Start LoRa broadcast if available
      if (await ref.read(loraServiceProvider).isAvailable()) {
        await ref.read(loraServiceProvider).broadcastAlert(alert);
      }
      
      // 7. Update state
      state = state.copyWith(
        isActive: true,
        isTriggering: false,
        currentAlert: alert,
        alertHistory: [...state.alertHistory, alert],
      );
      
      // 8. Start listening for guardian responses
      _listenForGuardianResponses(alert.id);
      
      // 9. Start battery conservation
      ref.read(batteryServiceProvider).enterEmergencyMode();
      
    } catch (e) {
      state = state.copyWith(isTriggering: false);
      // Handle failure - alert still queued locally
      _queueAlertForRetry();
    }
  }
  
  void _listenForGuardianResponses(String alertId) {
    ref.read(websocketProvider).listenForGuardianResponses(alertId, (response) {
      state = state.copyWith(lastGuardianResponse: DateTime.now());
      // Trigger "help coming" vibration pattern
      HapticFeedback.heavyImpact();
      Future.delayed(Duration(milliseconds: 100), () {
        HapticFeedback.heavyImpact();
      });
      Future.delayed(Duration(milliseconds: 200), () {
        HapticFeedback.heavyImpact();
      });
    });
  }
  
  Future<void> cancelAlert() async {
    if (!state.isActive) return;
    
    // Send cancellation to guardians
    await ref.read(alertRepositoryProvider).cancelAlert(state.currentAlert!.id);
    
    // Stop services
    await ref.read(audioServiceProvider).stopRecording();
    ref.read(batteryServiceProvider).exitEmergencyMode();
    
    state = state.copyWith(
      isActive: false,
      currentAlert: null,
    );
  }
  
  String _generateAlertId() {
    return 'ALT-${DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch}-${_randomString(6)}';
  }
  
  String _randomString(int length) {
    const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789';
    return List.generate(length, (index) => chars[Random().nextInt(chars.length)]).join();
  }
  
  Future<void> _loadHistory() async {
    final history = await ref.read(alertRepositoryProvider).getAlertHistory();
    state = state.copyWith(alertHistory: history);
  }
  
  Future<void> _queueAlertForRetry() async {
    // Store alert locally for retry when connectivity restores
    await ref.read(alertRepositoryProvider).queueAlert(state.currentAlert!);
  }
}
4.3 Platform Channels
dart
// services/platform/sms_platform.dart
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';

class SmsPlatformService {
  static const _channel = MethodChannel('com.aegis.sentinel/sms');
  static const _eventChannel = EventChannel('com.aegis.sentinel/sms_events');
  
  /// Send SMS with delivery confirmation
  Future<SmsResult> sendSms({
    required String phoneNumber,
    required String message,
    bool requireDeliveryReport = false,
  }) async {
    try {
      final result = await _channel.invokeMethod('sendSms', {
        'phoneNumber': phoneNumber,
        'message': message,
        'requireDeliveryReport': requireDeliveryReport,
      });
      
      return SmsResult(
        success: result['success'] as bool,
        messageId: result['messageId'] as String?,
        error: result['error'] as String?,
      );
    } on PlatformException catch (e) {
      return SmsResult(success: false, error: e.message);
    }
  }
  
  /// Send SMS to multiple recipients
  Future<List<SmsResult>> sendBulkSms({
    required List<String> phoneNumbers,
    required String message,
  }) async {
    final results = <SmsResult>[];
    for (final number in phoneNumbers) {
      results.add(await sendSms(phoneNumber: number, message: message));
    }
    return results;
  }
  
  /// Listen for incoming SMS (for guardian acknowledgement)
  Stream<SmsReceived> get onSmsReceived {
    return _eventChannel.receiveBroadcastStream().map((event) {
      return SmsReceived.fromMap(event as Map<String, dynamic>);
    });
  }
}

class SmsResult {
  final bool success;
  final String? messageId;
  final String? error;
  
  SmsResult({required this.success, this.messageId, this.error});
}

class SmsReceived {
  final String sender;
  final String message;
  final DateTime timestamp;
  
  SmsReceived({
    required this.sender,
    required this.message,
    required this.timestamp,
  });
  
  factory SmsReceived.fromMap(Map<String, dynamic> map) {
    return SmsReceived(
      sender: map['sender'] as String,
      message: map['message'] as String,
      timestamp: DateTime.fromMillisecondsSinceEpoch(map['timestamp'] as int),
    );
  }
}
4.4 Local Storage Architecture
dart
// data/local/database/app_database.dart
import 'package:drift/drift.dart';
import 'package:drift/native.dart';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'package:path/path.dart' as p;
import 'dart:io';

part 'app_database.g.dart';

// =============================================
// TABLE DEFINITIONS
// =============================================

class Alerts extends Table {
  TextColumn get id => text()();
  DateTimeColumn get triggerTime => dateTime()();
  RealColumn get latitude => real()();
  RealColumn get longitude => real()();
  IntColumn get guardiansNotified => integer()();
  BoolColumn get isActive => boolean()();
  BoolColumn get isCancelled => boolean()();
  DateTimeColumn get cancelledAt => dateTime().nullable()();
  TextColumn get status => text()(); // 'active', 'acknowledged', 'resolved', 'cancelled'
  
  @override
  Set<Column> get primaryKey => {id};
}

class Guardians extends Table {
  TextColumn get id => text()();
  TextColumn get name => text()();
  TextColumn get phoneNumber => text()();
  TextColumn get email => text().nullable()();
  BoolColumn get isPrimary => boolean()();
  BoolColumn get isActive => boolean()();
  DateTimeColumn get addedAt => dateTime()();
  DateTimeColumn get lastActive => dateTime().nullable()();
  TextColumn get relationship => text().nullable()(); // 'family', 'friend', 'colleague'
  
  @override
  Set<Column> get primaryKey => {id};
}

class LocationPoints extends Table {
  IntColumn get id => integer().autoIncrement()();
  RealColumn get latitude => real()();
  RealColumn get longitude => real()();
  RealColumn get accuracy => real()();
  RealColumn get altitude => real().nullable()();
  RealColumn get speed => real().nullable()();
  RealColumn get heading => real().nullable()();
  DateTimeColumn get timestamp => dateTime()();
  TextColumn get sessionType => text()(); // 'emergency', 'sentinel', 'journey', 'standard'
  TextColumn get alertId => text().nullable()();
  BoolColumn get isSynced => boolean().withDefault(const Constant(false))();
}

class DeviceScans extends Table {
  IntColumn get id => integer().autoIncrement()();
  TextColumn get sessionId => text()();
  DateTimeColumn get scanTime => dateTime()();
  TextColumn get deviceAddress => text()(); // Hashed MAC
  TextColumn get deviceName => text().nullable()();
  IntColumn get rssi => integer()();
  TextColumn get deviceType => text()(); // 'bluetooth', 'wifi', 'cellular'
  RealColumn get latitude => real()();
  RealColumn get longitude => real()();
  BoolColumn get isSynced => boolean().withDefault(const Constant(false))();
}

class AlertQueue extends Table {
  IntColumn get id => integer().autoIncrement()();
  TextColumn get alertId => text()();
  TextColumn get payload => text()(); // JSON payload
  IntColumn get retryCount => integer().withDefault(const Constant(0))();
  DateTimeColumn get createdAt => dateTime()();
  DateTimeColumn get lastRetry => dateTime().nullable()();
  DateTimeColumn get nextRetry => dateTime()();
  TextColumn get status => text()(); // 'pending', 'sending', 'sent', 'failed'
}

// =============================================
// DATABASE CLASS
// =============================================

@DriftDatabase(
  tables: [Alerts, Guardians, LocationPoints, DeviceScans, AlertQueue],
)
class AppDatabase extends _$AppDatabase {
  AppDatabase() : super(_openConnection());
  
  @override
  int get schemaVersion => 1;
  
  @override
  MigrationStrategy get migration => MigrationStrategy(
    onCreate: (m) async {
      await m.createAll();
    },
    onUpgrade: (m, from, to) async {
      // Handle migrations
    },
  );
  
  static QueryExecutor _openConnection() {
    return LazyDatabase(() async {
      final dbFolder = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
      final file = File(p.join(dbFolder.path, 'aegis.db'));
      return NativeDatabase.createInBackground(file);
    });
  }
  
  // =============================================
  // ALERT QUERIES
  // =============================================
  
  Future<void> insertAlert(Alert alert) => into(alerts).insert(alert);
  
  Future<List<Alert>> getActiveAlerts() {
    return (select(alerts)..where((t) => t.isActive.equals(true))).get();
  }
  
  Future<List<Alert>> getAlertHistory({int limit = 50}) {
    return (select(alerts)
      ..orderBy([(t) => OrderingTerm.desc(t.triggerTime)])
      ..limit(limit))
      .get();
  }
  
  Future<void> deactivateAlert(String alertId) {
    return (update(alerts)
      ..where((t) => t.id.equals(alertId)))
      .write(AlertsCompanion(
        isActive: const Value(false),
        cancelledAt: Value(DateTime.now()),
        status: const Value('cancelled'),
      ));
  }
  
  // =============================================
  // GUARDIAN QUERIES
  // =============================================
  
  Future<void> insertGuardian(Guardian guardian) => into(guardians).insert(guardian);
  
  Future<List<Guardian>> getActiveGuardians() {
    return (select(guardians)..where((t) => t.isActive.equals(true))).get();
  }
  
  Future<List<Guardian>> getPrimaryGuardians() {
    return (select(guardians)
      ..where((t) => t.isActive.equals(true) & t.isPrimary.equals(true)))
      .get();
  }
  
  // =============================================
  // LOCATION QUERIES
  // =============================================
  
  Future<void> insertLocationPoint(LocationPoint point) {
    return into(locationPoints).insert(point);
  }
  
  Future<List<LocationPoint>> getLocationsForSession(String sessionType, {int limit = 100}) {
    return (select(locationPoints)
      ..where((t) => t.sessionType.equals(sessionType))
      ..orderBy([(t) => OrderingTerm.desc(t.timestamp)])
      ..limit(limit))
      .get();
  }
  
  // =============================================
  // SCAN QUERIES
  // =============================================
  
  Future<void> insertScan(DeviceScan scan) => into(deviceScans).insert(scan);
  
  Future<int> getScanCountForSession(String sessionId) {
    return (selectOnly(deviceScans)
      ..addColumns([deviceScans.id.count()])
      ..where(deviceScans.sessionId.equals(sessionId)))
      .map((row) => row.read(deviceScans.id.count())!)
      .getSingle();
  }
  
  // =============================================
  // QUEUE QUERIES
  // =============================================
  
  Future<void> queueAlert(AlertQueue alert) => into(alertQueue).insert(alert);
  
  Future<List<AlertQueue>> getPendingAlerts() {
    return (select(alertQueue)
      ..where((t) => t.status.equals('pending') | t.status.equals('failed'))
      ..orderBy([(t) => OrderingTerm.asc(t.nextRetry)]))
      .get();
  }
}
5.0 iOS-Specific Implementation
5.1 iOS Configuration
swift
// ios/Runner/AppDelegate.swift
import UIKit
import Flutter
import UserNotifications
import CoreLocation
import AVFoundation
import BackgroundTasks

@UIApplicationMain
@objc class AppDelegate: FlutterAppDelegate, CLLocationManagerDelegate {
    
    private let locationManager = CLLocationManager()
    private var backgroundTask: UIBackgroundTaskIdentifier = .invalid
    
    override func application(
        _ application: UIApplication,
        didFinishLaunchingWithOptions launchOptions: [UIApplication.LaunchOptionsKey: Any]?
    ) -> Bool {
        GeneratedPluginRegistrant.register(with: self)
        
        // Configure notifications
        configureNotifications()
        
        // Configure location
        configureLocation()
        
        // Configure audio session
        configureAudioSession()
        
        // Register background tasks
        registerBackgroundTasks()
        
        return super.application(application, didFinishLaunchingWithOptions: launchOptions)
    }
    
    // MARK: - Notifications
    
    private func configureNotifications() {
        let center = UNUserNotificationCenter.current()
        center.delegate = self
        
        // Request critical alerts entitlement (bypasses Do Not Disturb)
        center.requestAuthorization(options: [.alert, .sound, .badge, .criticalAlert]) { granted, error in
            if granted {
                print("Notification authorization granted")
            }
        }
        
        // Define notification categories
        let emergencyCategory = UNNotificationCategory(
            identifier: "EMERGENCY_ALERT",
            actions: [
                UNNotificationAction(
                    identifier: "ACKNOWLEDGE",
                    title: "Acknowledge",
                    options: [.authenticationRequired, .foreground]
                ),
                UNNotificationAction(
                    identifier: "VIEW_MAP",
                    title: "View on Map",
                    options: .foreground
                )
            ],
            intentIdentifiers: [],
            options: [.customDismissAction]
        )
        
        center.setNotificationCategories([emergencyCategory])
    }
    
    // MARK: - Location
    
    private func configureLocation() {
        locationManager.delegate = self
        locationManager.desiredAccuracy = kCLLocationAccuracyBestForNavigation
        locationManager.distanceFilter = kCLDistanceFilterNone
        locationManager.allowsBackgroundLocationUpdates = true
        locationManager.pausesLocationUpdatesAutomatically = false
        locationManager.showsBackgroundLocationIndicator = true
        
        // Request always authorization for background updates
        locationManager.requestAlwaysAuthorization()
    }
    
    // CLLocationManagerDelegate
    func locationManager(_ manager: CLLocationManager, didUpdateLocations locations: [CLLocation]) {
        guard let location = locations.last else { return }
        
        // Send location to Flutter via method channel
        if let controller = window?.rootViewController as? FlutterViewController {
            let channel = FlutterMethodChannel(
                name: "com.aegis.sentinel/location",
                binaryMessenger: controller.binaryMessenger
            )
            
            channel.invokeMethod("onLocationUpdate", arguments: [
                "latitude": location.coordinate.latitude,
                "longitude": location.coordinate.longitude,
                "accuracy": location.horizontalAccuracy,
                "altitude": location.altitude,
                "speed": location.speed,
                "heading": location.course,
                "timestamp": location.timestamp.timeIntervalSince1970 * 1000
            ])
        }
    }
    
    // MARK: - Audio Session
    
    private func configureAudioSession() {
        let session = AVAudioSession.sharedInstance()
        do {
            // Configure for background recording
            try session.setCategory(
                .playAndRecord,
                mode: .voiceChat,
                options: [.allowBluetooth, .mixWithOthers, .defaultToSpeaker]
            )
            try session.setActive(true)
        } catch {
            print("Failed to configure audio session: \(error)")
        }
    }
    
    // MARK: - Background Tasks
    
    private func registerBackgroundTasks() {
        // Register sentinel scanning task
        BGTaskScheduler.shared.register(
            forTaskWithIdentifier: "com.aegis.sentinel.scan",
            using: nil
        ) { task in
            self.handleSentinelScan(task: task as! BGProcessingTask)
        }
        
        // Register location upload task
        BGTaskScheduler.shared.register(
            forTaskWithIdentifier: "com.aegis.sentinel.locationUpload",
            using: nil
        ) { task in
            self.handleLocationUpload(task: task as! BGProcessingTask)
        }
    }
    
    private func handleSentinelScan(task: BGProcessingTask) {
        // Schedule next scan
        scheduleSentinelScan()
        
        // Perform scan
        let channel = FlutterMethodChannel(
            name: "com.aegis.sentinel/background",
            binaryMessenger: (window?.rootViewController as! FlutterViewController).binaryMessenger
        )
        
        channel.invokeMethod("performBackgroundScan", arguments: nil) { result in
            task.setTaskCompleted(success: true)
        }
        
        // Handle expiration
        task.expirationHandler = {
            task.setTaskCompleted(success: false)
        }
    }
    
    private func handleLocationUpload(task: BGProcessingTask) {
        let channel = FlutterMethodChannel(
            name: "com.aegis.sentinel/background",
            binaryMessenger: (window?.rootViewController as! FlutterViewController).binaryMessenger
        )
        
        channel.invokeMethod("uploadQueuedData", arguments: nil) { result in
            task.setTaskCompleted(success: true)
        }
        
        task.expirationHandler = {
            task.setTaskCompleted(success: false)
        }
    }
    
    func scheduleSentinelScan() {
        let request = BGProcessingTaskRequest(identifier: "com.aegis.sentinel.scan")
        request.requiresNetworkConnectivity = false
        request.requiresExternalPower = false
        request.earliestBeginDate = Date(timeIntervalSinceNow: 60) // 1 minute
        
        do {
            try BGTaskScheduler.shared.submit(request)
        } catch {
            print("Failed to schedule sentinel scan: \(error)")
        }
    }
    
    // MARK: - Lifecycle
    
    override func applicationDidEnterBackground(_ application: UIApplication) {
        // Start background task
        backgroundTask = application.beginBackgroundTask(withName: "AegisBackground") {
            application.endBackgroundTask(self.backgroundTask)
            self.backgroundTask = .invalid
        }
        
        // Schedule background tasks
        scheduleSentinelScan()
    }
    
    override func applicationWillEnterForeground(_ application: UIApplication) {
        // End background task
        if backgroundTask != .invalid {
            application.endBackgroundTask(backgroundTask)
            backgroundTask = .invalid
        }
    }
    
    override func applicationWillTerminate(_ application: UIApplication) {
        // Save any pending data
        if let controller = window?.rootViewController as? FlutterViewController {
            let channel = FlutterMethodChannel(
                name: "com.aegis.sentinel/lifecycle",
                binaryMessenger: controller.binaryMessenger
            )
            channel.invokeMethod("onTerminate", arguments: nil)
        }
    }
}

5.4 iOS-Specific Features
swift
// ios/Runner/SiriIntents.swift
import Intents
import CoreLocation

/// Siri Shortcuts for Aegis Sentinel
/// Users can say "Hey Siri, I need help" to trigger emergency
class EmergencyIntentHandler: NSObject, INIntentHandlerProviding {
    
    func handler(for intent: INIntent) -> Any? {
        if intent is INEmergencyIntent {
            return EmergencyIntentHandler()
        }
        return nil
    }
}

extension EmergencyIntentHandler: INEmergencyIntentHandling {
    
    func handle(intent: INEmergencyIntent, completion: @escaping (INEmergencyIntentResponse) -> Void) {
        // Trigger emergency via Flutter method channel
        if let controller = (UIApplication.shared.delegate as? AppDelegate)?
            .window?.rootViewController as? FlutterViewController {
            
            let channel = FlutterMethodChannel(
                name: "com.aegis.sentinel/siri",
                binaryMessenger: controller.binaryMessenger
            )
            
            channel.invokeMethod("triggerEmergencyFromSiri", arguments: nil) { result in
                let response = INEmergencyIntentResponse(
                    code: .success,
                    userActivity: nil
                )
                response.alertSent = true
                completion(response)
            }
        }
    }
}

/// iOS 16+ Lock Screen Widget
import WidgetKit
import SwiftUI

struct EmergencyWidget: Widget {
    let kind: String = "EmergencyWidget"
    
    var body: some WidgetConfiguration {
        StaticConfiguration(kind: kind, provider: Provider()) { entry in
            EmergencyWidgetEntryView(entry: entry)
        }
        .configurationDisplayName("Emergency")
        .description("Quick access to emergency alert.")
        .supportedFamilies([.accessoryCircular, .accessoryRectangular])
    }
}

struct EmergencyWidgetEntryView: View {
    var entry: Provider.Entry
    
    var body: some View {
        if #available(iOS 16.0, *) {
            Button(intent: TriggerEmergencyIntent()) {
                Image(systemName: "shield.fill")
                    .font(.system(size: 24))
                    .foregroundColor(.red)
            }
            .buttonStyle(.plain)
        }
    }
}
6.0 Testing Requirements
6.1 Critical Test Scenarios
Test ID	Scenario	Expected Result	Platform
T-001	User triggers alert with full connectivity	Alert reaches guardians < 3s, SMS sent, audio streaming begins	Both
T-002	User triggers alert with no data (SMS only)	SMS delivered, app queues HTTP, retries when connectivity restores	Both
T-003	User triggers alert with no GSM (LoRa only)	LoRa broadcast sent, mesh relays to nearest internet-connected node	Both
T-004	User triggers alert with phone locked	Alert functions from lock screen widget/button sequence	Both
T-005	User triggers alert while app is in disguise mode	Alert functions, notepad appearance maintained	Both
T-006	Guardian receives alert while phone is in silent mode	Alert overrides silent mode (critical notification)	Both
T-007	Guardian receives alert while phone is in Do Not Disturb	Alert bypasses DND (critical notification)	Both
T-008	Multiple simultaneous alerts (load test)	No degradation, each alert processed independently	Both
T-009	GPS unavailable (indoors, bad weather)	Falls back to network location, accuracy noted in payload	Both
T-010	Battery at 5%	Alert still functions, optimized sensor usage	Both
T-011	App killed by OS	Background service restarts, alert queue preserved	iOS
T-012	App killed by user (force stop)	Alert queue preserved, service restarts on next boot	Android
T-013	Device reboot during emergency	Alert resumes on boot, guardians notified of gap	Both
T-014	Siri trigger while phone locked	Emergency alert sent, requires FaceID/TouchID bypass	iOS
T-015	Apple Watch companion trigger	Alert sent via watch, phone relays with full data	iOS
T-016	Airplane mode activation during emergency	SMS/LoRa still attempted, data queued	Both




# 03 - Guardian Web Dashboard

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Platform:** Web (PWA), Mobile-responsive
- **Framework:** Next.js 14, React 18, TailwindCSS

---

## 1.0 Overview

The Guardian Dashboard is the interface for emergency contacts who receive alerts. It must function flawlessly under stress, on any device, with any connection quality.

### 1.1 Design Principles
- **Clarity over aesthetics** - information must be instantly parseable
- **Progressive loading** - core map and alert first, secondary data streams second
- **Offline resilience** - PWA with service worker caching
- **Multi-device sync** - state shared across guardian devices

---

## 2.0 UI Specification

### 2.1 Alert Reception Screen (Critical UX)

\`\`\`
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  🚨 EMERGENCY ALERT                           Aegis CSG     │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

│  │                                                        │ │

### 2.4 Technical Implementation

\`\`\`typescript
// pages/alert/[id].tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import dynamic from 'next/dynamic';
import { AlertProvider, useAlert } from '@/contexts/AlertContext';
import { GuardianProvider } from '@/contexts/GuardianContext';
import { WebSocketProvider } from '@/contexts/WebSocketContext';

// Dynamically import heavy components
const LiveMap = dynamic(() => import('@/components/maps/LiveMap'), {
  ssr: false,
  loading: () => <MapSkeleton />
});

const AudioStream = dynamic(() => import('@/components/AudioStream'), {
  ssr: false
});

export default function AlertPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { id } = router.query;
  
  return (
    <AlertProvider alertId={id as string}>
      <WebSocketProvider>
        <GuardianProvider>
          <AlertDashboard />
        </GuardianProvider>
      </WebSocketProvider>
    </AlertProvider>
  );
}

function AlertDashboard() {
  const { alert, victim, location, acknowledge } = useAlert();
  const [isAcknowledging, setIsAcknowledging] = useState(false);
  
  const handleAcknowledge = async () => {
    setIsAcknowledging(true);
    try {
      await acknowledge();
      // Trigger haptic/audio feedback
      if ('vibrate' in navigator) {
        navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]); // Pattern: "Alert received"
      }
    } finally {
      setIsAcknowledging(false);
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-900 text-white">
      {/* Critical Alert Banner */}
      <div className="bg-red-600 px-4 py-3 animate-pulse">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex items-center justify-between">
          <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
            <ExclamationIcon className="h-8 w-8" />
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">EMERGENCY ALERT</h1>
              <p className="text-sm opacity-90">{victim?.name} needs immediate assistance</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="text-right">
            <p className="text-sm">Alert received</p>
            <p className="text-lg font-mono">{alert?.elapsedTime}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto p-4 grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        {/* Map - Takes 2/3 width on desktop */}
        <div className="lg:col-span-2">
          <div className="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg overflow-hidden h-[60vh]">
            <LiveMap
              victimLocation={location}
              guardianLocations={alert?.guardians}
              riskOverlay={true}
            />
          </div>
          
          {/* Location Timeline */}
          <LocationTimeline points={alert?.locationHistory} />
        </div>
        
        {/* Side Panel */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {/* Victim Info Card */}
          <VictimInfoCard victim={victim} alert={alert} />
          
          {/* Audio Stream */}
          <AudioStream streamUrl={alert?.audioStreamUrl} />
          
          {/* Action Buttons */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
            <button
              onClick={handleAcknowledge}
              disabled={isAcknowledging}
              className="bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700 disabled:bg-gray-600 
                         text-white font-bold py-4 px-6 rounded-lg
                         transition-all duration-200 transform hover:scale-105"
            >
              {isAcknowledging ? 'Sending...' : '✅ ACKNOWLEDGE'}
            </button>
            
            <a
              href={`tel:${emergencyNumbers.police}`}
              className="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white font-bold 
                         py-4 px-6 rounded-lg text-center transition-all"
            >
              📞 CALL POLICE
            </a>
          </div>
          
          {/* Guardian Chat */}
          <GuardianChat alertId={alert?.id} />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
\`\`\`

## 3.0 PWA Configuration

\`\`\`typescript
// next.config.js
const withPWA = require('next-pwa')({
  dest: 'public',
  register: true,
  skipWaiting: true,
  disable: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development',
  runtimeCaching: [
    {
      urlPattern: /^https:\/\/api\.aegis\.ng\/.*$/,
      handler: 'NetworkFirst',
      options: {
        cacheName: 'api-cache',
        expiration: {
          maxEntries: 100,
          maxAgeSeconds: 60 * 60, // 1 hour
        },
      },
    },
    {
      urlPattern: /^https:\/\/tiles\.aegis\.ng\/.*$/,
      handler: 'CacheFirst',
      options: {
        cacheName: 'map-tiles',
        expiration: {
          maxEntries: 500,
          maxAgeSeconds: 60 * 60 * 24 * 30, // 30 days
        },
      },
    },
  ],
});

module.exports = withPWA({
  reactStrictMode: true,
  images: {
    domains: ['api.aegis.ng', 'cdn.aegis.ng'],
  },
});
\`\`\`

# 04 - Security Forces Command Center

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0 Production
- **Platform:** Web (React/Next.js), Progressive Web App
- **Users:** Police, Civil Defense, Military (authorized)
- **Classification:** Restricted - Law Enforcement Only
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Overview

The Command Center is the operational interface for security forces responding to alerts. It provides situational awareness, resource coordination, and intelligence analysis tools designed for high-stakes, time-critical operations.

### 1.1 Design Principles
- **Action-First Design:** Every screen optimized for immediate decision-making
- **Progressive Disclosure:** Show critical info first, drill down for details
- **Persistence:** All state preserved across browser crashes and reconnections
- **Multi-Modal:** Works on desktop, tablet, and mobile for field commanders
- **Offline-Ready:** Core functions work on degraded connections

### 1.2 Access Tiers & Permissions

| Tier | Role | Capabilities | Authentication |
|------|------|--------------|----------------|
| **Watch Officer** | Duty officers monitoring alerts | View active alerts, acknowledge, dispatch initial response | Password + TOTP |
| **Commander** | Shift commanders, area commanders | Full operational control, resource allocation, escalation | Password + Hardware Key (YubiKey) |
| **Analyst** | Intelligence analysts | Access to historical data, pattern analysis, ML model training | Password + TOTP + IP whitelist |
| **Administrator** | System administrators | User management, audit log review, system configuration | Hardware Key + Biometric |
| **Super Admin** | NITDA/Civil Society oversight | Read-only access to anonymized data, audit trails | Multi-party authorization (4-eyes) |

---

## 3.0 Technical Implementation

### 3.1 Technology Stack

```typescript
// package.json
{
  "name": "@aegis/command-center",
  "version": "2.0.0",
  "private": true,
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "next dev -p 3001",
    "build": "next build",
    "start": "next start",
    "analyze": "ANALYZE=true next build",
    "lint": "eslint . --ext .ts,.tsx",
    "type-check": "tsc --noEmit",
    "test": "jest --passWithNoTests",
    "test:e2e": "playwright test"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "next": "^14.1.0",
    "react": "^18.2.0",
    "react-dom": "^18.2.0",
    "typescript": "^5.3.0",
    
    // UI Framework
    "@radix-ui/react-dialog": "^1.0.5",
    "@radix-ui/react-dropdown-menu": "^2.0.6",
    "@radix-ui/react-tabs": "^1.0.4",
    "@radix-ui/react-toast": "^1.1.5",
    "@radix-ui/react-tooltip": "^1.0.7",
    "tailwindcss": "^3.4.0",
    "lucide-react": "^0.312.0",
    
    // Maps
    "maplibre-gl": "^3.6.0",
    "@maplibre/maplibre-gl-geocoder": "^1.5.0",
    "react-map-gl": "^7.1.0",
    
    // Real-time
    "socket.io-client": "^4.7.0",

3.2 Core Components
typescript
// components/operations/OperationsMap.tsx
import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback, useState } from 'react';
import maplibregl from 'maplibre-gl';
import 'maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl.css';
import { useAlertsStore } from '@/stores/alerts';
import { useUnitsStore } from '@/stores/units';
import { useRiskStore } from '@/stores/risk';
import { useWebSocket } from '@/hooks/useWebSocket';
import type { Alert, Unit, RiskZone } from '@/types';

interface OperationsMapProps {
  onAlertClick: (alert: Alert) => void;
  selectedAlert: Alert | null;
}

export const OperationsMap: React.FC<OperationsMapProps> = ({
  onAlertClick,
  selectedAlert,
}) => {
  const mapContainer = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const map = useRef<maplibregl.Map | null>(null);
  const [isMapLoaded, setIsMapLoaded] = useState(false);
  
  const alerts = useAlertsStore((s) => s.activeAlerts);
  const units = useUnitsStore((s) => s.units);
  const riskZones = useRiskStore((s) => s.zones);
  
  // Initialize map
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapContainer.current || map.current) return;
    
    map.current = new maplibregl.Map({
      container: mapContainer.current,
      style: 'https://tiles.aegis.ng/styles/command-center/style.json',
      center: [7.4356, 10.5234], // Kaduna center
      zoom: 11,
      minZoom: 6,
      maxZoom: 18,
      attributionControl: false,
    });
    
    map.current.addControl(new maplibregl.NavigationControl(), 'top-left');
    map.current.addControl(new maplibregl.ScaleControl(), 'bottom-left');
    
    map.current.on('load', () => {
      setIsMapLoaded(true);
      addCustomLayers();
    });
    
    return () => {
      map.current?.remove();
    };
  }, []);
  
  // Add custom data layers
  const addCustomLayers = useCallback(() => {
    if (!map.current) return;
    
    // Risk heatmap layer
    map.current.addSource('risk-heatmap', {
      type: 'geojson',
      data: {
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: riskZones.map(zone => ({
          type: 'Feature',
          geometry: {
            type: 'Polygon',
            coordinates: zone.polygon,
          },
          properties: {
            riskScore: zone.score,
            riskLevel: zone.level,
          },
        })),
      },
    });
    
    map.current.addLayer({
      id: 'risk-heatmap-fill',
      type: 'fill',
      source: 'risk-heatmap',
      paint: {
        'fill-color': [
          'interpolate',
          ['linear'],
          ['get', 'riskScore'],
          0, '#00ff00',
          0.25, '#ffff00',
          0.5, '#ffaa00',
          0.75, '#ff4400',
          1.0, '#ff0000',
        ],
        'fill-opacity': 0.3,
      },
    });
    
    // Alert markers layer
    map.current.addSource('active-alerts', {
      type: 'geojson',
      data: {
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: [],
      },
    });
    
    map.current.addLayer({
      id: 'alert-markers',
      type: 'circle',
      source: 'active-alerts',
      paint: {
        'circle-radius': [
          'interpolate',
          ['linear'],
          ['get', 'minutesSinceAlert'],
          0, 20,
          30, 15,
          60, 10,
        ],
        'circle-color': [
          'match',
          ['get', 'priority'],
          'critical', '#ff0000',
          'high', '#ff4400',
          'medium', '#ffaa00',
          'low', '#ffff00',
          '#cccccc',
        ],
        'circle-stroke-width': 2,
        'circle-stroke-color': '#ffffff',
        'circle-opacity': 0.9,
      },
    });
    
    // Click handler for alerts
    map.current.on('click', 'alert-markers', (e) => {
      if (e.features && e.features[0]) {
        const alertId = e.features[0].properties?.id;
        const alert = alerts.find(a => a.id === alertId);
        if (alert) {
          onAlertClick(alert);
        }
      }
    });
    
    // Cursor change on hover
    map.current.on('mouseenter', 'alert-markers', () => {
      map.current!.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
    });
    map.current.on('mouseleave', 'alert-markers', () => {
      map.current!.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';
    });
    
  }, [riskZones, alerts, onAlertClick]);
  
  // Update alert markers when alerts change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!map.current || !isMapLoaded) return;
    
    const source = map.current.getSource('active-alerts') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource;
    if (!source) return;
    
    source.setData({
      type: 'FeatureCollection',
      features: alerts.map(alert => ({
        type: 'Feature',
        geometry: {
          type: 'Point',
          coordinates: [alert.longitude, alert.latitude],
        },
        properties: {
          id: alert.id,
          minutesSinceAlert: Math.floor(
            (Date.now() - alert.triggerTime.getTime()) / 60000
          ),
          priority: alert.priority,
          victimName: alert.victimName,
        },
      })),
    });
  }, [alerts, isMapLoaded]);
  
  // Fly to selected alert
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!map.current || !selectedAlert) return;
    
    map.current.flyTo({
      center: [selectedAlert.longitude, selectedAlert.latitude],
      zoom: 15,
      duration: 1500,
    });
  }, [selectedAlert]);
  
  return (
    <div className="relative w-full h-full">
      <div ref={mapContainer} className="w-full h-full" />
      
      {/* Layer Toggle Panel */}
      <div className="absolute top-4 right-4 bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-3 z-10">
        <LayerToggles />
      </div>
      
      {/* Time Slider */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-4 right-4 bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-3 z-10">
        <TimeSlider />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
3.3 WebSocket Real-Time Updates
typescript
// hooks/useWebSocket.ts
import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client';
import { useAlertsStore } from '@/stores/alerts';
import { useUnitsStore } from '@/stores/units';
import { useAuthStore } from '@/stores/auth';

const WS_URL = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_WS_URL || 'wss://api.aegis.ng/command';

export const useWebSocket = () => {
  const socketRef = useRef<Socket | null>(null);
  const token = useAuthStore((s) => s.token);
  const addAlert = useAlertsStore((s) => s.addAlert);
  const updateAlert = useAlertsStore((s) => s.updateAlert);
  const updateUnitLocation = useUnitsStore((s) => s.updateUnitLocation);
  
  const connect = useCallback(() => {
    if (!token) return;
    
    const socket = io(WS_URL, {
      auth: { token },
      transports: ['websocket'],
      reconnection: true,
      reconnectionDelay: 1000,
      reconnectionDelayMax: 30000,
      reconnectionAttempts: Infinity,
    });
    
    socket.on('connect', () => {
      console.log('[WS] Connected to Command Center');
      
      // Join region rooms based on user's jurisdiction
      socket.emit('join:region', 'north-central');
    });
    
    socket.on('alert:new', (alert) => {
      addAlert(alert);
      
      // Trigger audio alert for critical alerts
      if (alert.priority === 'critical') {
        playCriticalAlertSound();
      }
    });
    
    socket.on('alert:update', (update) => {
      updateAlert(update.id, update);
    });
    
    socket.on('alert:resolved', (alertId) => {
      updateAlert(alertId, { status: 'resolved', resolvedAt: new Date() });
    });
    
    socket.on('unit:location', (data) => {
      updateUnitLocation(data.unitId, {
        latitude: data.latitude,
        longitude: data.longitude,
        heading: data.heading,
        speed: data.speed,
      });
    });
    
    socket.on('disconnect', (reason) => {
      console.warn('[WS] Disconnected:', reason);
    });
    
    socket.on('error', (error) => {
      console.error('[WS] Error:', error);
    });
    
    socketRef.current = socket;
  }, [token, addAlert, updateAlert, updateUnitLocation]);
  
  const disconnect = useCallback(() => {
    socketRef.current?.disconnect();
    socketRef.current = null;
  }, []);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    connect();
    return () => disconnect();
  }, [connect, disconnect]);
  
  return {
    socket: socketRef.current,
    reconnect: connect,
  };
};

function playCriticalAlertSound() {
  const audio = new Audio('/sounds/critical-alert.mp3');
  audio.volume = 0.8;
  audio.play().catch(() => {
    // Browser may block autoplay
  });
}
3.4 State Management (Zustand)
typescript
// stores/alerts.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import type { Alert, AlertUpdate } from '@/types';

interface AlertsState {
  activeAlerts: Alert[];
  selectedAlertId: string | null;
  filters: {
    priority: string[];
    status: string[];
    region: string | null;
  };
  
  // Actions
  addAlert: (alert: Alert) => void;
  updateAlert: (id: string, update: Partial<AlertUpdate>) => void;
  resolveAlert: (id: string) => void;
  selectAlert: (id: string | null) => void;
  setFilters: (filters: Partial<AlertsState['filters']>) => void;
  
  // Selectors
  getSelectedAlert: () => Alert | null;
  getFilteredAlerts: () => Alert[];
  getCriticalAlerts: () => Alert[];
}

export const useAlertsStore = create<AlertsState>()(
  immer(
    persist(
      (set, get) => ({
        activeAlerts: [],
        selectedAlertId: null,
        filters: {
          priority: ['critical', 'high', 'medium', 'low'],
          status: ['active'],
          region: null,
        },
        
        addAlert: (alert) =>
          set((state) => {
            // Check for duplicate
            const exists = state.activeAlerts.find((a) => a.id === alert.id);
            if (!exists) {
              state.activeAlerts.unshift(alert);
            }
          }),
        
        updateAlert: (id, update) =>
          set((state) => {
            const alert = state.activeAlerts.find((a) => a.id === id);
            if (alert) {
              Object.assign(alert, update);
            }
          }),
        
        resolveAlert: (id) =>
          set((state) => {
            const alert = state.activeAlerts.find((a) => a.id === id);
            if (alert) {
              alert.status = 'resolved';
              alert.resolvedAt = new Date();
            }
            if (state.selectedAlertId === id) {
              state.selectedAlertId = null;
            }
          }),
        
        selectAlert: (id) =>
          set((state) => {
            state.selectedAlertId = id;
          }),
        
        setFilters: (filters) =>
          set((state) => {
            Object.assign(state.filters, filters);
          }),
        
        getSelectedAlert: () => {
          const state = get();
          return state.activeAlerts.find((a) => a.id === state.selectedAlertId) ?? null;
        },
        
        getFilteredAlerts: () => {
          const state = get();
          return state.activeAlerts.filter((a) => {
            if (!state.filters.priority.includes(a.priority)) return false;
            if (!state.filters.status.includes(a.status)) return false;
            if (state.filters.region && a.region !== state.filters.region) return false;
            return true;
          });
        },
        
        getCriticalAlerts: () => {
          return get().activeAlerts.filter((a) => a.priority === 'critical');
        },
      }),
      {
        name: 'aegis-alerts-store',
        partialize: (state) => ({
          activeAlerts: state.activeAlerts,
        }),
      }
    )
  )
);

5.0 Security Requirements
5.1 Authentication Flow
typescript
// auth/authenticate.ts
import { getServerSession } from 'next-auth';
import { verifyAuthenticationResponse } from '@simplewebauthn/server';
import type { NextAuthOptions } from 'next-auth';

export const authOptions: NextAuthOptions = {
  providers: [
    {
      id: 'webauthn',
      name: 'Security Key',
      type: 'credentials',
      credentials: {},
      async authorize(credentials, req) {
        // WebAuthn verification
        const authenticationResponse = JSON.parse(
          req.body?.authenticationResponse || '{}'
        );
        
        const verification = await verifyAuthenticationResponse({
          response: authenticationResponse,
          expectedChallenge: req.body?.challenge,
          expectedOrigin: process.env.NEXTAUTH_URL,
          expectedRPID: 'aegis.ng',
          authenticator: {
            // Stored authenticator data
            credentialPublicKey: new Uint8Array(),
            credentialID: new Uint8Array(),
            counter: 0,
          },
        });
        
        if (!verification.verified) {
          return null;
        }
        
        // Get user from database
        const user = await getUserByCredentialId(verification.authInfo.credentialID);
        
        // Check authorization level
        if (!user || !user.isAuthorized) {
          return null;
        }
        
        return {
          id: user.id,
          name: user.name,
          role: user.role,
          region: user.region,
        };
      },
    },
  ],
  session: {
    strategy: 'jwt',
    maxAge: 8 * 60 * 60, // 8 hours - matches typical shift
  },
  callbacks: {
    async jwt({ token, user }) {
      if (user) {
        token.role = user.role;
        token.region = user.region;
      }
      return token;
    },
    async session({ session, token }) {
      session.user.role = token.role;
      session.user.region = token.region;
      return session;
    },
  },
  pages: {
    signIn: '/auth/signin',
    error: '/auth/error',
  },
};
5.2 Audit Logging
typescript
// lib/audit.ts
import { prisma } from './prisma';
import type { AuditAction } from '@/types';

interface AuditLogEntry {
  userId: string;
  action: AuditAction;
  resourceType: string;
  resourceId: string;
  details: Record<string, any>;
  ipAddress: string;
  userAgent: string;
}

export async function logAuditEvent(entry: AuditLogEntry): Promise<void> {
  await prisma.auditLog.create({
    data: {
      userId: entry.userId,
      action: entry.action,
      resourceType: entry.resourceType,
      resourceId: entry.resourceId,
      details: entry.details,
      ipAddress: entry.ipAddress,
      userAgent: entry.userAgent,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    },
  });
  
  // For sensitive actions, also write to immutable blockchain log
  if (isSensitiveAction(entry.action)) {
    await writeToBlockchain(entry);
  }
}

function isSensitiveAction(action: AuditAction): boolean {
  return [
    'VIEW_VICTIM_PII',
    'EXPORT_DATA',
    'DISPATCH_UNIT',
    'RESOLVE_ALERT',
    'MODIFY_SETTINGS',
  ].includes(action);
}

async function writeToBlockchain(entry: AuditLogEntry): Promise<void> {
  // Submit to Hyperledger Fabric
  await fetch(`${process.env.FABRIC_API}/invoke`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      channel: 'audit',
      chaincode: 'audit_log',
      method: 'LogEvent',
      args: [
        entry.userId,
        entry.action,
        entry.resourceType,
        entry.resourceId,
        JSON.stringify(entry.details),
        entry.timestamp.toISOString(),
      ],
    }),
  });
}
6.0 Notification System
6.1 Alert Escalation Logic
typescript
// lib/escalation.ts
import { sendPushNotification } from './notifications';
import { sendSMS } from './sms';
import { logAuditEvent } from './audit';

interface EscalationRule {
  condition: (alert: Alert) => boolean;
  action: (alert: Alert) => Promise<void>;
  priority: number;
}

const escalationRules: EscalationRule[] = [
  {
    // Critical alert with no guardian acknowledgement after 2 minutes
    condition: (alert) => 
      alert.priority === 'critical' && 
      alert.guardiansAcknowledged === 0 &&
      alert.elapsedMinutes > 2,
    action: async (alert) => {
      await notifyOnCallCommander(alert);
      await logAuditEvent({
        userId: 'system',
        action: 'ESCALATION_TRIGGERED',
        resourceType: 'alert',
        resourceId: alert.id,
        details: { reason: 'No guardian response after 2 minutes' },
        ipAddress: 'system',
        userAgent: 'system',
      });
    },
    priority: 1,
  },
  {
    // Alert moving into known high-risk area
    condition: (alert) =>
      alert.isMoving &&
      isInHighRiskZone(alert.currentLocation) &&
      alert.elapsedMinutes > 5,
    action: async (alert) => {
      await escalateToRegionalCommander(alert);
      await recommendCheckpointAlert(alert);
    },
    priority: 2,
  },
  {
    // Battery critically low while alert active
    condition: (alert) =>
      alert.batteryLevel < 10 &&
      alert.status === 'active',
    action: async (alert) => {
      await notifyGuardiansOfImpendingDisconnection(alert);
      await increaseLocationPollingFrequency(alert.id);
    },
    priority: 3,
  },
];

export async function evaluateEscalations(alert: Alert): Promise<void> {
  const applicableRules = escalationRules
    .filter(rule => rule.condition(alert))
    .sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
  
  for (const rule of applicableRules) {
    await rule.action(alert);
  }
}
7.0 Offline Resilience
7.1 Service Worker Strategy
typescript
// service-worker.ts
import { precacheAndRoute } from 'workbox-precaching';
import { registerRoute } from 'workbox-routing';
import { NetworkFirst, CacheFirst, StaleWhileRevalidate } from 'workbox-strategies';
import { ExpirationPlugin } from 'workbox-expiration';
import { BackgroundSyncPlugin } from 'workbox-background-sync';

// Precache critical assets
precacheAndRoute(self.__WB_MANIFEST);

// API calls - Network First, fallback to cache
registerRoute(
  ({ url }) => url.pathname.startsWith('/api/'),
  new NetworkFirst({
    cacheName: 'api-cache',
    plugins: [
      new ExpirationPlugin({
        maxEntries: 100,
        maxAgeSeconds: 5 * 60, // 5 minutes
      }),
    ],
  })
);

// Map tiles - Cache First
registerRoute(
  ({ url }) => url.hostname === 'tiles.aegis.ng',
  new CacheFirst({
    cacheName: 'map-tiles',
    plugins: [
      new ExpirationPlugin({
        maxEntries: 1000,
        maxAgeSeconds: 30 * 24 * 60 * 60, // 30 days
      }),
    ],
  })
);

// Alert actions - Queue when offline
const alertSync = new BackgroundSyncPlugin('alert-actions-queue', {
  maxRetentionTime: 24 * 60, // Retry for up to 24 hours
});

registerRoute(
  ({ url }) => url.pathname.startsWith('/api/alerts/') && url.pathname.includes('/action'),
  new NetworkFirst({
    cacheName: 'alert-actions',
    plugins: [alertSync],
  }),
  'POST'
);

8.1 Critical Test Scenarios
Test ID	Scenario	Expected Result
CC-001	Critical alert received, commander dispatches unit	Unit receives dispatch order within 5 seconds, appears on map
CC-002	Multiple simultaneous critical alerts	All alerts visible, no UI degradation, escalation rules evaluate independently
CC-003	Network disconnection during alert monitoring	UI continues to show last known state, queues actions for sync
CC-004	Unauthorized user attempts PII access	Access denied, audit log recorded, security alert triggered
CC-005	Alert resolution workflow	Alert marked resolved, all data archived, guardians notified

## 1.0 System Architecture

### 1.1 Core Components

\`\`\`
┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

## 2.0 Data Pipeline

### 2.1 Event Ingestion

\`\`\`python
# event_ingestor.py
from kafka import KafkaConsumer
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional, List
import json

class SensorEvent(BaseModel):
    device_id: str
    event_type: str  # 'alert', 'scan', 'location_update'
    timestamp: int
    location: tuple[float, float]
    data: dict
    
class EventIngestor:
    def __init__(self, kafka_brokers: List[str]):
        self.consumer = KafkaConsumer(
            'sensor-events',
            bootstrap_servers=kafka_brokers,
            value_deserializer=lambda m: json.loads(m.decode('utf-8')),
            group_id='oracle-ingestor',
            auto_offset_reset='latest',
            enable_auto_commit=False,
            max_poll_records=500,
        )
        
    async def process_events(self):
        for message in self.consumer:
            event = SensorEvent(**message.value)
            
            # Route to appropriate processor
            if event.event_type == 'alert':
                await self.process_alert(event)
            elif event.event_type == 'scan':
                await self.process_scan(event)
            elif event.event_type == 'location_update':
                await self.process_location(event)
            
            # Commit offset after successful processing
            self.consumer.commit()
            
    async def process_alert(self, event: SensorEvent):
        # Validate alert authenticity
        if not await self.validate_alert(event):
            return
            
        # Write to graph database
        await self.graph_service.create_alert_node(event)
        
        # Trigger real-time anomaly check
        await self.anomaly_detector.check_alert_context(event)
        
        # Update risk scores
        await self.risk_engine.update_from_alert(event)
        
    async def process_scan(self, event: SensorEvent):
        # Anonymize and aggregate scan data
        anonymized = self.privacy_service.anonymize_scan(event.data)
        
        # Check for device density anomalies
        await self.anomaly_detector.check_device_density(
            event.location, 
            anonymized
        )
        
        # Update device graph
        await self.graph_service.update_device_graph(anonymized)
\`\`\`

### 2.2 Anomaly Detection Models

\`\`\`python
# anomaly_detector.py
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from typing import List, Tuple
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class SpatialTemporalAnomalyDetector:
    """
    Detects anomalies in device density and movement patterns.
    Uses ensemble of models for robustness.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.isolation_forest = IsolationForest(
            contamination=0.1,
            random_state=42
        )
        self.autoencoder = self._build_autoencoder()
        self.threshold_model = self._build_threshold_model()
        
    def _build_autoencoder(self) -> nn.Module:
        """Autoencoder for detecting unusual patterns in device signatures."""
        class Autoencoder(nn.Module):
            def __init__(self):
                super().__init__()
                self.encoder = nn.Sequential(
                    nn.Linear(128, 64),
                    nn.ReLU(),
                    nn.Linear(64, 32),
                    nn.ReLU(),
                    nn.Linear(32, 16),
                )
                self.decoder = nn.Sequential(
                    nn.Linear(16, 32),
                    nn.ReLU(),
                    nn.Linear(32, 64),
                    nn.ReLU(),
                    nn.Linear(64, 128),
                )
                
            def forward(self, x):
                encoded = self.encoder(x)
                decoded = self.decoder(encoded)
                return decoded
                
        return Autoencoder()
    
    def check_device_density(
        self, 
        location: Tuple[float, float], 
        current_devices: List[dict],
        time_window: timedelta = timedelta(hours=1)
    ) -> float:
        """
        Check if current device density is anomalous for this location and time.
        
        Returns:
            float: Anomaly score (0.0 = normal, 1.0 = highly anomalous)
        """
        # Get historical baseline for this grid cell and time
        grid_cell = self.grid_service.get_cell(location)
        baseline = self.baseline_service.get_density_baseline(
            grid_cell, 
            datetime.now(), 
            time_window
        )
        
        # Extract features
        current_density = len(current_devices)
        new_device_ratio = len([d for d in current_devices if d['is_new']]) / max(current_density, 1)
        time_of_day = datetime.now().hour
        day_of_week = datetime.now().weekday()
        
        features = np.array([
            current_density,
            new_device_ratio,
            time_of_day,
            day_of_week,
            baseline.mean_density,
            baseline.std_density,
        ]).reshape(1, -1)
        
        # Ensemble scoring
        if_score = self.isolation_forest.score_samples(features)[0]
        
        # Normalize to 0-1 range
        anomaly_score = 1.0 - (1.0 / (1.0 + np.exp(-if_score)))
        
        return anomaly_score
    
    def check_movement_pattern(
        self,
        device_path: List[Tuple[float, float, int]]
    ) -> float:
        """
        Detect suspicious movement patterns (e.g., circling, sudden stops on highways).
        """
        # Extract movement features
        speeds = self._calculate_speeds(device_path)
        accelerations = self._calculate_accelerations(speeds)
        path_efficiency = self._calculate_path_efficiency(device_path)
        
        features = torch.tensor([
            np.mean(speeds),
            np.std(speeds),
            np.max(accelerations),
            path_efficiency,
        ], dtype=torch.float32)
        
        # Autoencoder reconstruction error
        with torch.no_grad():
            reconstructed = self.autoencoder(features)
            reconstruction_error = nn.MSELoss()(reconstructed, features)
            
        return reconstruction_error.item()
    
    def _calculate_speeds(self, path):
        speeds = []
        for i in range(1, len(path)):
            lat1, lon1, t1 = path[i-1]
            lat2, lon2, t2 = path[i]
            distance = self._haversine(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2)
            time_diff = (t2 - t1) / 3600  # hours
            if time_diff > 0:
                speeds.append(distance / time_diff)  # km/h
        return speeds
    
    def _haversine(self, lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2):
        """Calculate distance between two GPS coordinates in km."""
        R = 6371  # Earth radius in km
        dlat = np.radians(lat2 - lat1)
        dlon = np.radians(lon2 - lon1)
        a = (np.sin(dlat/2)**2 + 
             np.cos(np.radians(lat1)) * 
             np.cos(np.radians(lat2)) * 
             np.sin(dlon/2)**2)
        c = 2 * np.arctan2(np.sqrt(a), np.sqrt(1-a))
        return R * c
\`\`\`

### 2.3 Graph-Based Relationship Discovery

\`\`\`python
# graph_engine.py
from neo4j import AsyncGraphDatabase
from typing import List, Dict
import asyncio

class GraphEngine:
    """
    Manages the Neo4j graph database for relationship mapping and discovery.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, uri: str, user: str, password: str):
        self.driver = AsyncGraphDatabase.driver(uri, auth=(user, password))
        
    async def find_suspicious_clusters(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """
        Discover clusters of devices that appear together across multiple incidents.
        This is a key capability for identifying kidnapping rings.
        """
        async with self.driver.session() as session:
            result = await session.run("""
                // Find device clusters that co-occur in multiple alert zones
                MATCH (d1:Device)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc:GridCell)<-[:DETECTED_AT]-(d2:Device)
                WHERE d1 <> d2
                AND gc.risk_score > 0.7
                
                // Count co-occurrences
                WITH d1, d2, count(gc) as co_occurrences
                WHERE co_occurrences >= 3
                
                // Find the grid cells where they co-occur
                MATCH (d1)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc1:GridCell)
                MATCH (d2)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc2:GridCell)
                WHERE gc1 = gc2
                
                RETURN 
                    d1.mac_address as device1,
                    d2.mac_address as device2,
                    co_occurrences,
                    collect(gc1.id) as locations
                ORDER BY co_occurrences DESC
                LIMIT 100
            """)
            
            return [record.data() for record in await result.consume()]
    
    async def trace_device_movement(self, device_mac: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """
        Trace the movement history of a specific device across the grid.
        """
        async with self.driver.session() as session:
            result = await session.run("""
                MATCH (d:Device {mac_address: $mac})-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc:GridCell)
                OPTIONAL MATCH (gc)<-[:OCCURRED_IN]-(a:Alert)
                RETURN 
                    gc.id as grid_cell,
                    gc.centroid_lat as lat,
                    gc.centroid_lng as lng,
                    collect(DISTINCT a) as alerts
                ORDER BY gc.id
            """, mac=device_mac)
            
            records = []
            async for record in result:
                records.append(record.data())
            
            return records
    
    async def find_anomalous_device_groups(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """
        Identify groups of devices that appear together with unusual patterns.
        Uses community detection algorithms.
        """
        async with self.driver.session() as session:
            # Project graph for GDS algorithms
            await session.run("""
                CALL gds.graph.project(
                    'device-network',
                    'Device',
                    {
                        CO_OCCURS: {
                            type: 'DETECTED_AT',
                            orientation: 'UNDIRECTED'
                        }
                    }
                )
            """)
            
            # Run Louvain community detection
            result = await session.run("""
                CALL gds.louvain.stream('device-network')
                YIELD nodeId, communityId
                WITH gds.util.asNode(nodeId) AS device, communityId
                WHERE device.suspicious_score > 0.5
                RETURN 
                    communityId,
                    collect(device.mac_address) as devices,
                    count(*) as group_size
                ORDER BY group_size DESC
                LIMIT 20
            """)
            
            return [record.data() for record in await result.consume()]
    
    async def close(self):
        await self.driver.close()

### 2.4 Risk Scoring Engine

\`\`\`python
# risk_engine.py
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, Tuple

class RiskScoringEngine:
    """
    Calculates real-time risk scores for geographic grid cells.
    Combines multiple signals into a unified risk assessment.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, graph_engine, anomaly_detector):
        self.graph = graph_engine
        self.anomaly = anomaly_detector
        
        # Risk factor weights (tunable)
        self.weights = {
            'historical_incidents': 0.30,
            'device_density_anomaly': 0.20,
            'temporal_pattern': 0.15,
            'movement_anomaly': 0.15,
            'community_reports': 0.10,
            'proximity_to_active_alerts': 0.10,
        }
        
    async def calculate_grid_risk(
        self, 
        grid_cell_id: str,
        timestamp: datetime = None
    ) -> float:
        """
        Calculate composite risk score for a grid cell.
        
        Returns:
            float: Risk score 0.0 (safe) to 1.0 (critical)
        """
        if timestamp is None:
            timestamp = datetime.now()
            
        scores = {}
        
        # Historical incident density
        scores['historical_incidents'] = await self._historical_incident_score(
            grid_cell_id, timestamp
        )
        
        # Current device density anomaly
        scores['device_density_anomaly'] = await self._density_anomaly_score(
            grid_cell_id
        )
        
        # Temporal pattern (time-of-day risk)
        scores['temporal_pattern'] = self._temporal_risk_score(timestamp)
        
        # Movement anomalies
        scores['movement_anomaly'] = await self._movement_anomaly_score(
            grid_cell_id
        )
        
        # Community reports
        scores['community_reports'] = await self._community_report_score(
            grid_cell_id
        )
        
        # Proximity to active alerts
        scores['proximity_to_active_alerts'] = await self._proximity_score(
            grid_cell_id
        )
        
        # Weighted combination
        composite_score = sum(
            scores[factor] * self.weights[factor]
            for factor in self.weights
        )
        
        return min(max(composite_score, 0.0), 1.0)
    
    async def _historical_incident_score(self, grid_id: str, timestamp: datetime):
        """Score based on historical incidents in this grid cell."""
        # Query for incidents in last 90 days
        incidents = await self.graph.get_incidents_in_grid(
            grid_id, 
            timestamp - timedelta(days=90),
            timestamp
        )
        
        if not incidents:
            return 0.0
            
        # Exponential decay for older incidents
        scores = []
        for incident in incidents:
            days_ago = (timestamp - incident.timestamp).days
            decay = np.exp(-days_ago / 30)  # Half-life of ~21 days
            scores.append(decay * incident.severity)
            
        return min(sum(scores) / 10, 1.0)  # Normalize
    
    async def _density_anomaly_score(self, grid_id: str):
        """Current device density anomaly score."""
        current_devices = await self.graph.get_current_devices(grid_id)
        anomaly_score = self.anomaly.check_device_density(
            grid_id, 
            current_devices
        )
        return anomaly_score
    
    def _temporal_risk_score(self, timestamp: datetime):
        """Risk based on time patterns (kidnappings spike at certain times)."""
        hour = timestamp.hour
        
        # Known high-risk periods (based on Nigeria kidnapping data)
        if 22 <= hour or hour <= 4:  # Night (10 PM - 4 AM)
            return 0.8
        elif 18 <= hour <= 21:  # Evening
            return 0.6
        elif 5 <= hour <= 7:  # Early morning
            return 0.4
        else:
            return 0.2

| Data Type | Minimum Volume | Preferred Volume | Source |

| Device density scans | 100,000 | 1,000,000+ | Sentinel Mode users |
| Movement trajectories | 10,000 | 100,000+ | Journey Mode users |
| Community reports | 1,000 | 10,000+ | App user reports |

### 3.2 Model Architecture for Prediction

\`\`\`python
# predictive_model.py
import torch
import torch.nn as nn

class KidnapRiskPredictor(nn.Module):
    """
    Predicts kidnapping risk for a given location and time window.
    Uses spatial-temporal transformer architecture.
    """
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        input_dim: int = 64,
        hidden_dim: int = 256,
        num_heads: int = 8,
        num_layers: int = 4,
        dropout: float = 0.1
    ):
        super().__init__()
        
        # Spatial encoder (location features)
        self.spatial_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(2, 32),  # lat, lng
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(32, 64),
            nn.ReLU(),
        )
        
        # Temporal encoder (time features)
        self.temporal_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(4, 32),  # hour, day, month, is_weekend
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(32, 64),
        )
        
        # Device density encoder
        self.density_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(10, 64),  # density features
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 64),
        )
        
        # Transformer for pattern recognition
        encoder_layer = nn.TransformerEncoderLayer(
            d_model=hidden_dim,
            nhead=num_heads,
            dropout=dropout,
            batch_first=True
        )
        self.transformer = nn.TransformerEncoder(
            encoder_layer, 
            num_layers=num_layers
        )
        
        # Output head
        self.output_head = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(hidden_dim, 128),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Dropout(dropout),
            nn.Linear(128, 64),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 1),
            nn.Sigmoid()  # Risk probability
        )
        
    def forward(self, spatial, temporal, density, historical):
        # Encode inputs
        s_emb = self.spatial_encoder(spatial)
        t_emb = self.temporal_encoder(temporal)
        d_emb = self.density_encoder(density)
        
        # Combine embeddings
        combined = torch.cat([
            s_emb.unsqueeze(1),
            t_emb.unsqueeze(1),
            d_emb.unsqueeze(1),
            historical
        ], dim=1)
        
        # Process through transformer
        transformed = self.transformer(combined)
        
        # Global pooling
        pooled = transformed.mean(dim=1)
        
        # Output risk probability
        risk = self.output_head(pooled)
        
        return risk

## 4.0 API Endpoints

\`\`\`python
# api.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Depends
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Optional

app = FastAPI(title="Oracle Engine API", version="2.0")

class RiskAssessmentRequest(BaseModel):
    latitude: float
    longitude: float
    timestamp: Optional[int] = None
    route: Optional[List[tuple[float, float]]] = None

class RiskAssessmentResponse(BaseModel):
    grid_cell_id: str
    risk_score: float
    risk_level: str  # 'low', 'moderate', 'high', 'critical'
    factors: dict
    recommendations: List[str]

@app.post("/api/v2/risk/assess", response_model=RiskAssessmentResponse)
async def assess_risk(request: RiskAssessmentRequest):
    """
    Assess risk for a specific location. Used by Sentinel App for:
    - Route planning
    - Real-time risk display
    - Sentinel Mode activation suggestions
    """
    risk_engine = get_risk_engine()
    
    score = await risk_engine.calculate_location_risk(
        request.latitude,
        request.longitude
    )
    
    return RiskAssessmentResponse(
        grid_cell_id=f"grid_{int(request.latitude)}_{int(request.longitude)}",
        risk_score=score,
        risk_level=get_risk_level(score),
        factors=await risk_engine.get_contributing_factors(
            request.latitude,
            request.longitude
        ),
        recommendations=generate_recommendations(score),
    )

class AnomalyReportRequest(BaseModel):
    device_id: str
    scan_data: dict
    location: tuple[float, float]

@app.post("/api/v2/anomaly/report")
async def report_anomaly(request: AnomalyReportRequest):
    """Endpoint for Sentinel Mode devices to submit scan data."""
    anomaly_detector = get_anomaly_detector()
    
    score = await anomaly_detector.check_device_density(
        request.location,
        request.scan_data.get('devices', [])
    )
    
    return {
        "anomaly_score": score,
        "threshold_exceeded": score > 0.7,
        "action_required": score > 0.85,
    }

# 06 - AegisNet LoRaWAN Mesh Network

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0 Production
- **Hardware:** Heltec WiFi LoRa 32 V3 / Custom ESP32-S3
- **Firmware:** C++ (Arduino/PlatformIO)
- **Backend:** ChirpStack / Custom MQTT Bridge
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Overview

AegisNet is the decentralized communication backbone that functions when GSM networks are unavailable or compromised. It uses LoRa (Long Range) radio technology operating in the 868 MHz ISM band (license-free in Nigeria) to create a self-healing mesh network of community-deployed nodes.

### 1.1 Design Principles
- **Decentralized:** No single node failure brings down the network
- **Self-Healing:** Automatic rerouting around damaged nodes
- **Low Power:** Solar-powered, indefinite operation without grid electricity
- **Stealth:** Nodes appear as innocuous weather stations or utility boxes
- **Open Protocol:** Based on LoRaWAN for interoperability

---

## 2.0 Network Architecture

### 2.1 Topology
INTERNET BACKHAUL
│
┌──────────┴──────────┐
│ │
┌─────▼─────┐ ┌─────▼─────┐
│ Gateway │ │ Gateway │
│ Node A │ │ Node B │
│ (WiFi/4G) │ │ (WiFi/4G) │
└─────┬─────┘ └─────┬─────┘
│ │
┌──────────┼─────────┬───────────┼──────────┐
│ │ │ │ │
┌────▼────┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐
│ Relay │ │ Relay │ │ Relay │ │ Relay │ │ Relay │
│ Node 1 │ │Node 2 │ │Node 3 │ │Node 4 │ │Node 5 │
└────┬────┘ └───┬───┘ └───┬───┘ └───┬───┘ └───┬───┘
│ │ │ │ │
┌────▼────┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐ ┌───▼───┐
│ End │ │ End │ │ End │ │ End │ │ End │
│ Node │ │ Node │ │ Node │ │ Node │ │ Node │
└─────────┘ └───────┘ └───────┘ └───────┘ └───────┘

Gateway Nodes: Internet-connected, mains/solar powered
Relay Nodes: Mesh routers, solar powered, no internet
End Nodes: Sentinel App phones with LoRa capability (future)

text

### 2.2 Node Types

| Type | Hardware | Power | Range | Function |
|------|----------|-------|-------|----------|
| **Gateway** | Heltec LoRa 32 V3 + Raspberry Pi | Mains + Solar backup | 10-15 km | Internet backhaul, MQTT bridge |
| **Relay** | Heltec LoRa 32 V3 | Solar + 18650 battery | 5-10 km | Mesh routing, packet forwarding |
| **Community Hub** | Raspberry Pi 4 + LoRa HAT | Solar + 18650 | 5-10 km | Local processing, offline Neo4j |
| **End Node** | Smartphone with external LoRa | Phone battery | 1-3 km | Personal emergency beacon |
