## 4.0 Firmware Specification

### 4.1 Gateway Firmware

```cpp
// gateway_firmware.ino
#include <SPI.h>
#include <LoRa.h>
#include <WiFi.h>
#include <PubSubClient.h>
#include <ArduinoJson.h>
#include <AES.h>
#include <time.h>

// =============================================
// CONFIGURATION
// =============================================
#define LORA_FREQUENCY 868E6      // 868 MHz for Nigeria
#define LORA_BANDWIDTH 125E3      // 125 kHz
#define LORA_SPREADING_FACTOR 7   // SF7 (faster, shorter range)
#define LORA_CODING_RATE 5        // 4/5
#define LORA_TX_POWER 20          // 20 dBm (max for Heltec)

#define WIFI_SSID "AegisNet_Config"
#define WIFI_PASSWORD ""           // Will be set during deployment

#define MQTT_BROKER "mqtt.aegis.ng"
#define MQTT_PORT 8883            // TLS
#define MQTT_TOPIC_ALERTS "aegisnet/alerts"
#define MQTT_TOPIC_SCANS "aegisnet/scans"
#define MQTT_TOPIC_HEARTBEAT "aegisnet/heartbeat"

// Encryption key (provisioned during deployment)
uint8_t AES_KEY[32] = {0};  // 256-bit key
uint8_t AES_IV[16] = {0};   // Initialization vector

// =============================================
// GLOBAL OBJECTS
// =============================================
WiFiClientSecure wifiClient;
PubSubClient mqttClient(wifiClient);
AES256 aes;

// Statistics
struct {
  uint32_t packetsReceived = 0;
  uint32_t packetsForwarded = 0;
  uint32_t packetsDropped = 0;
  uint32_t alertsRelayed = 0;
  uint32_t lastHeartbeat = 0;
} stats;

// Message queue for offline buffering
#define QUEUE_SIZE 100
String messageQueue[QUEUE_SIZE];
uint8_t queueHead = 0;
uint8_t queueTail = 0;
uint8_t queueCount = 0;

// =============================================
// SETUP
// =============================================
void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  while (!Serial && millis() < 5000);
  
  Serial.println(F("[AEGISNET] Gateway Node Starting..."));
  
  // Initialize LoRa
  if (!initLoRa()) {
    Serial.println(F("[ERROR] LoRa initialization failed!"));
    // Blink LED rapidly to indicate error
    while (1) {
      digitalWrite(LED_BUILTIN, !digitalRead(LED_BUILTIN));
      delay(100);
    }
  }
  
  // Initialize WiFi
  initWiFi();
  
  // Initialize MQTT
  initMQTT();
  
  // Load encryption keys from secure storage
  loadEncryptionKeys();
  
  // Initialize NTP for timestamp
  configTime(0, 0, "pool.ntp.org", "time.nist.gov");
  
  Serial.println(F("[AEGISNET] Gateway Node Ready"));
  Serial.printf("  LoRa Frequency: %.2f MHz\n", LORA_FREQUENCY / 1E6);
  Serial.printf("  Node ID: %s\n", getNodeId().c_str());
}

// =============================================
// MAIN LOOP
// =============================================
void loop() {
  // Process incoming LoRa packets
  processLoRaPackets();
  
  // Maintain MQTT connection
  if (!mqttClient.connected()) {
    reconnectMQTT();
  }
  mqttClient.loop();
  
  // Process queued messages (from offline period)
  processMessageQueue();
  
  // Send heartbeat
  if (millis() - stats.lastHeartbeat > 60000) { // Every 60 seconds
    sendHeartbeat();
    stats.lastHeartbeat = millis();
  }
  
  // LED status
  updateStatusLED();
}

// =============================================
// LORA FUNCTIONS
// =============================================
bool initLoRa() {
  SPI.begin(18, 19, 23, 18); // SCK, MISO, MOSI, SS
  LoRa.setPins(18, 14, 26);  // SS, RST, DIO0
  
  if (!LoRa.begin(LORA_FREQUENCY)) {
    return false;
  }
  
  // Configure LoRa parameters
  LoRa.setSpreadingFactor(LORA_SPREADING_FACTOR);
  LoRa.setSignalBandwidth(LORA_BANDWIDTH);
  LoRa.setCodingRate4(LORA_CODING_RATE);
  LoRa.setTxPower(LORA_TX_POWER);
  LoRa.enableCrc();
  
  // Register callback for received packets
  LoRa.onReceive(onLoRaReceive);
  LoRa.receive(); // Put in receive mode
  
  return true;
}

void onLoRaReceive(int packetSize) {
  if (packetSize == 0) return;
  
  stats.packetsReceived++;
  
  // Read packet
  String receivedData = "";
  while (LoRa.available()) {
    receivedData += (char)LoRa.read();
  }
  
  // Get RSSI and SNR
  int rssi = LoRa.packetRssi();
  float snr = LoRa.packetSnr();
  
  // Parse packet
  StaticJsonDocument<512> doc;
  DeserializationError error = deserializeJson(doc, receivedData);
  
  if (error) {
    Serial.printf("[WARN] Failed to parse LoRa packet: %s\n", error.c_str());
    stats.packetsDropped++;
    return;
  }
  
  // Validate packet
  if (!validatePacket(doc)) {
    stats.packetsDropped++;
    return;
  }
  
  // Decrypt payload
  String payload = doc["payload"];
  String decryptedPayload = decryptPayload(payload);
  
  // Route based on packet type
  String packetType = doc["type"];
  
  if (packetType == "alert") {
    handleAlertPacket(decryptedPayload, rssi, snr);
  } else if (packetType == "scan") {
    handleScanPacket(decryptedPayload, rssi, snr);
  } else if (packetType == "heartbeat") {
    handleHeartbeatPacket(decryptedPayload, rssi);
  }
  
  // Forward if TTL > 0 (mesh routing)
  int ttl = doc["ttl"] | 3;
  if (ttl > 1) {
    doc["ttl"] = ttl - 1;
    forwardPacket(doc);
  }
}

void handleAlertPacket(String payload, int rssi, float snr) {
  // This is an emergency alert - HIGHEST PRIORITY
  
  // Parse alert data
  StaticJsonDocument<512> alertDoc;
  deserializeJson(alertDoc, payload);
  
  // Add metadata
  alertDoc["rssi"] = rssi;
  alertDoc["snr"] = snr;
  alertDoc["gateway_id"] = getNodeId();
  alertDoc["timestamp"] = getTimestamp();
  
  // Serialize for MQTT
  String mqttPayload;
  serializeJson(alertDoc, mqttPayload);
  
  // Publish immediately (skip queue for alerts)
  if (mqttClient.connected()) {
    mqttClient.publish(MQTT_TOPIC_ALERTS, mqttPayload.c_str());
  } else {
    // Queue for later - but mark as priority
    enqueueMessage("PRIORITY:" + mqttPayload);
  }
  
  stats.alertsRelayed++;
  
  // Flash LED rapidly to indicate alert relayed
  for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
    digitalWrite(LED_BUILTIN, HIGH);
    delay(50);
    digitalWrite(LED_BUILTIN, LOW);
    delay(50);
  }
}

void handleScanPacket(String payload, int rssi, float snr) {
  // This is a Sentinel Mode scan - batch with others
  
  StaticJsonDocument<512> scanDoc;
  deserializeJson(scanDoc, payload);
  
  scanDoc["rssi"] = rssi;
  scanDoc["snr"] = snr;
  scanDoc["gateway_id"] = getNodeId();
  
  String mqttPayload;
  serializeJson(scanDoc, mqttPayload);
  
  // Publish or queue
  if (mqttClient.connected()) {
    mqttClient.publish(MQTT_TOPIC_SCANS, mqttPayload.c_str());
  } else {
    enqueueMessage(mqttPayload);
  }
}

bool forwardPacket(JsonDocument& doc) {
  String forwardData;
  serializeJson(doc, forwardData);
  
  // Small random delay to avoid collisions
  delay(random(0, 100));
  
  LoRa.beginPacket();
  LoRa.print(forwardData);
  bool success = LoRa.endPacket();
  
  if (success) {
    stats.packetsForwarded++;
  }
  
  return success;
}

// =============================================
// ENCRYPTION FUNCTIONS
// =============================================
String encryptPayload(String plaintext) {
  // AES-256-CBC encryption
  int len = plaintext.length();
  int paddedLen = ((len / 16) + 1) * 16;
  uint8_t* input = (uint8_t*)malloc(paddedLen);
  uint8_t* output = (uint8_t*)malloc(paddedLen);
  
  memset(input, 0, paddedLen);
  memcpy(input, plaintext.c_str(), len);
  
  // PKCS7 padding
  uint8_t padLen = paddedLen - len;
  for (int i = len; i < paddedLen; i++) {
    input[i] = padLen;
  }
  
  aes.encrypt(input, paddedLen, output, AES_KEY, 256, AES_IV);
  
  // Base64 encode
  String encrypted = base64Encode(output, paddedLen);
  
  free(input);
  free(output);
  
  return encrypted;
}

String decryptPayload(String encrypted) {
  // Base64 decode
  int decodedLen = 0;
  uint8_t* decoded = base64Decode(encrypted, &decodedLen);
  
  uint8_t* plaintext = (uint8_t*)malloc(decodedLen);
  aes.decrypt(decoded, decodedLen, plaintext, AES_KEY, 256, AES_IV);
  
  // Remove PKCS7 padding
  uint8_t padLen = plaintext[decodedLen - 1];
  int plainLen = decodedLen - padLen;
  
  String result = String((char*)plaintext).substring(0, plainLen);
  
  free(decoded);
  free(plaintext);
  
  return result;
}

bool validatePacket(JsonDocument& doc) {
  // Check required fields
  if (!doc.containsKey("type")) return false;
  if (!doc.containsKey("payload")) return false;
  if (!doc.containsKey("node_id")) return false;
  if (!doc.containsKey("signature")) return false;
  
  // Verify signature (HMAC-SHA256)
  String payload = doc["payload"];
  String signature = doc["signature"];
  String expectedSig = computeHMAC(payload);
  
  if (signature != expectedSig) {
    Serial.println(F("[SECURITY] Invalid packet signature! Possible spoofing attempt."));
    return false;
  }
  
  return true;
}

// =============================================
// WIFI & MQTT FUNCTIONS
// =============================================
void initWiFi() {
  WiFi.begin(WIFI_SSID, WIFI_PASSWORD);
  
  Serial.print(F("[WiFi] Connecting"));
  int attempts = 0;
  while (WiFi.status() != WL_CONNECTED && attempts < 30) {
    delay(1000);
    Serial.print(".");
    attempts++;
  }
  
  if (WiFi.status() == WL_CONNECTED) {
    Serial.println(F("\n[WiFi] Connected"));
    Serial.printf("  IP: %s\n", WiFi.localIP().toString().c_str());
  } else {
    Serial.println(F("\n[WiFi] Failed to connect - operating in relay mode"));
  }
}

void initMQTT() {
  wifiClient.setInsecure(); // For development; use proper CA in production
  
  mqttClient.setServer(MQTT_BROKER, MQTT_PORT);
  mqttClient.setCallback(onMQTTMessage);
}

void reconnectMQTT() {
  if (!WiFi.isConnected()) return;
  
  int attempts = 0;
  while (!mqttClient.connected() && attempts < 3) {
    Serial.print(F("[MQTT] Connecting..."));
    
    String clientId = "aegisnet-gateway-" + getNodeId();
    if (mqttClient.connect(clientId.c_str())) {
      Serial.println(F(" connected"));
      mqttClient.subscribe("aegisnet/command/#");
    } else {
      Serial.printf(" failed (rc=%d). Retrying...\n", mqttClient.state());
      delay(5000);
    }
    attempts++;
  }
}

void onMQTTMessage(char* topic, byte* payload, unsigned int length) {
  // Handle commands from command center
  String topicStr = String(topic);
  String payloadStr = String((char*)payload).substring(0, length);
  
  Serial.printf("[MQTT] Received: %s -> %s\n", topic, payloadStr);
  
  if (topicStr == "aegisnet/command/restart") {
    ESP.restart();
  } else if (topicStr == "aegisnet/command/test_alert") {
    // Send test alert back to verify connectivity
    sendHeartbeat();
  }
}

// =============================================
// MESSAGE QUEUE (Offline Buffering)
// =============================================
void enqueueMessage(String message) {
  if (queueCount >= QUEUE_SIZE) {
    Serial.println(F("[WARN] Message queue full, dropping oldest message"));
    queueHead = (queueHead + 1) % QUEUE_SIZE;
    queueCount--;
  }
  
  messageQueue[queueTail] = message;
  queueTail = (queueTail + 1) % QUEUE_SIZE;
  queueCount++;
}

void processMessageQueue() {
  if (!mqttClient.connected()) return;
  if (queueCount == 0) return;
  
  Serial.printf("[QUEUE] Processing %d queued messages...\n", queueCount);
  
  while (queueCount > 0) {
    String message = messageQueue[queueHead];
    queueHead = (queueHead + 1) % QUEUE_SIZE;
    queueCount--;
    
    bool isPriority = message.startsWith("PRIORITY:");
    if (isPriority) {
      message = message.substring(9); // Remove prefix
      mqttClient.publish(MQTT_TOPIC_ALERTS, message.c_str());
    } else {
      mqttClient.publish(MQTT_TOPIC_SCANS, message.c_str());
    }
    
    delay(50); // Avoid flooding broker
  }
  
  Serial.println(F("[QUEUE] All messages processed"));
}

// =============================================
// HEARTBEAT & STATUS
// =============================================
void sendHeartbeat() {
  StaticJsonDocument<256> doc;
  doc["type"] = "heartbeat";
  doc["node_id"] = getNodeId();
  doc["node_type"] = "gateway";
  doc["uptime"] = millis() / 1000;
  doc["packets_received"] = stats.packetsReceived;
  doc["packets_forwarded"] = stats.packetsForwarded;
  doc["alerts_relayed"] = stats.alertsRelayed;
  doc["queue_size"] = queueCount;
  doc["wifi_rssi"] = WiFi.RSSI();
  doc["free_heap"] = ESP.getFreeHeap();
  doc["timestamp"] = getTimestamp();
  
  String payload;
  serializeJson(doc, payload);
  
  if (mqttClient.connected()) {
    mqttClient.publish(MQTT_TOPIC_HEARTBEAT, payload.c_str());
  }
}

void updateStatusLED() {
  // Status LED patterns:
  // - Solid: Normal operation, connected
  // - Slow blink: Normal operation, no internet (relay only)
  // - Fast blink: Alert being relayed
  // - Very fast blink: Error
  
  if (!WiFi.isConnected()) {
    // Slow blink - relay mode
    digitalWrite(LED_BUILTIN, (millis() / 1000) % 2);
  } else {
    // Solid - connected
    digitalWrite(LED_BUILTIN, HIGH);
  }
}

// =============================================
// UTILITY FUNCTIONS
// =============================================
String getNodeId() {
  // Use ESP32 MAC address as node ID
  uint8_t mac[6];
  WiFi.macAddress(mac);
  char id[13];
  snprintf(id, 13, "%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X", 
           mac[0], mac[1], mac[2], mac[3], mac[4], mac[5]);
  return String(id);
}

String getTimestamp() {
  time_t now;
  struct tm timeinfo;
  if (!getLocalTime(&timeinfo)) {
    return String(millis());
  }
  char timestamp[30];
  strftime(timestamp, 30, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", &timeinfo);
  return String(timestamp);
}

String computeHMAC(String data) {
  // HMAC-SHA256 using pre-shared key
  // Implementation using mbedtls
  uint8_t hmac[32];
  mbedtls_md_context_t ctx;
  mbedtls_md_type_t md_type = MBEDTLS_MD_SHA256;
  
  mbedtls_md_init(&ctx);
  mbedtls_md_setup(&ctx, mbedtls_md_info_from_type(md_type), 1);
  mbedtls_md_hmac_starts(&ctx, AES_KEY, 32);
  mbedtls_md_hmac_update(&ctx, (const unsigned char*)data.c_str(), data.length());
  mbedtls_md_hmac_finish(&ctx, hmac);
  mbedtls_md_free(&ctx);
  
  return base64Encode(hmac, 32);
}

String base64Encode(uint8_t* data, int len) {
  // Simple base64 encoding
  const char* base64chars = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
  String result = "";
  for (int i = 0; i < len; i += 3) {
    int b = (data[i] & 0xFC) >> 2;
    result += base64chars[b];
    // ... full implementation
  }
  return result;
}

void loadEncryptionKeys() {
  // In production, load from ESP32's encrypted NVS (Non-Volatile Storage)
  // For now, use hardcoded keys (REPLACE IN PRODUCTION)
  const uint8_t defaultKey[32] = {
    0x00, 0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04, 0x05, 0x06, 0x07,
    0x08, 0x09, 0x0A, 0x0B, 0x0C, 0x0D, 0x0E, 0x0F,
    0x10, 0x11, 0x12, 0x13, 0x14, 0x15, 0x16, 0x17,
    0x18, 0x19, 0x1A, 0x1B, 0x1C, 0x1D, 0x1E, 0x1F
  };
  memcpy(AES_KEY, defaultKey, 32);
}
5.0 Community Hub Software
python
# community_hub.py
"""
Runs on Raspberry Pi at community level.
Provides local processing when internet is unavailable.
"""

import asyncio
import json
from datetime import datetime
from neo4j import AsyncGraphDatabase
from paho.mqtt import client as mqtt
import sqlite3
import os

class CommunityHub:
    def __init__(self, node_id: str):
        self.node_id = node_id
        self.neo4j = None
        self.mqtt_client = None
        self.local_db = None
        
    async def initialize(self):
        # Initialize local Neo4j (Community Edition on Pi)
        self.neo4j = AsyncGraphDatabase.driver(
            "bolt://localhost:7687",
            auth=("neo4j", os.getenv("NEO4J_PASSWORD"))
        )
        
        # Initialize local SQLite for queued data
        self.local_db = sqlite3.connect("aegis_local.db")
        self._create_tables()
        
        # Initialize MQTT for upstream sync
        self.mqtt_client = mqtt.Client(f"hub-{self.node_id}")
        self.mqtt_client.on_connect = self._on_mqtt_connect
        self.mqtt_client.connect("mqtt.aegis.ng", 8883)
        self.mqtt_client.loop_start()
        
    def _create_tables(self):
        self.local_db.execute("""
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS queued_alerts (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                payload TEXT,
                created_at TIMESTAMP,
                synced INTEGER DEFAULT 0
            )
        """)
        self.local_db.execute("""
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS queued_scans (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                payload TEXT,
                created_at TIMESTAMP,
                synced INTEGER DEFAULT 0
            )
        """)
        self.local_db.commit()
        
    async def process_local_alert(self, alert_data: dict):
        """Process alert locally when offline, queue for sync."""
        # Store in local Neo4j
        async with self.neo4j.session() as session:
            await session.run("""
                CREATE (a:Alert {
                    id: $id,
                    latitude: $lat,
                    longitude: $lng,
                    timestamp: datetime($time),
                    victim_id: $victim
                })
            """, alert_data)
        
        # Queue for upstream sync
        self.local_db.execute(
            "INSERT INTO queued_alerts VALUES (?, ?, ?, 0)",
            (alert_data['id'], json.dumps(alert_data), datetime.now())
        )
        self.local_db.commit()
        
        # If MQTT connected, try to sync immediately
        if self.mqtt_client.is_connected():
            await self.sync_queued_data()
    
    async def sync_queued_data(self):
        """Sync queued data to central servers."""
        unsynced = self.local_db.execute(
            "SELECT * FROM queued_alerts WHERE synced = 0"
        ).fetchall()
        
        for row in unsynced:
            self.mqtt_client.publish("aegisnet/alerts", row[1])
            self.local_db.execute(
                "UPDATE queued_alerts SET synced = 1 WHERE id = ?",
                (row[0],)
            )
        
        self.local_db.commit()

# Run the hub
hub = CommunityHub("hub-kaduna-01")
asyncio.run(hub.initialize())
6.0 Deployment Guide
6.1 Site Survey Checklist
Line of sight to at least one other node

Elevated position (rooftop, pole, tree)

Solar exposure (south-facing for northern hemisphere)

Physical security (tamper-resistant mounting)

Distance from GSM towers (to avoid interference)

Community acceptance (explain purpose to local leaders)

6.2 Installation Procedure
Pre-configure node with unique ID and encryption keys

Mount enclosure at surveyed location

Connect antenna and ensure clear sky view

Position solar panel for optimal exposure

Power on and verify heartbeat on network dashboard

Test emergency relay from test Sentinel device

Document GPS coordinates for network map

End of AegisNet Mesh Complete Documentation




# 07 - Pillar Immutable Evidence Ledger

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0 Production
- **Platform:** Hyperledger Fabric 2.5
- **Language:** Go (Chaincode), Node.js (API)
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Overview

Pillar is a permissioned blockchain that serves as the immutable evidence log and transparency backbone for Aegis CSG. It provides:
- Tamper-proof evidence custody chain
- Transparent, auditable alert logging
- Public verification of system integrity
- Privacy-preserving data sharing between authorized parties

### 1.1 Why Permissioned Blockchain?

| Requirement | Public Blockchain | Permissioned (Hyperledger) |
|-------------|-------------------|---------------------------|
| Data privacy | ❌ All data public | ✅ Private data collections |
| Transaction speed | ❌ Minutes (confirmation) | ✅ Sub-second |
| Energy consumption | ❌ High (PoW) | ✅ Minimal (RAFT) |
| Regulatory compliance | ❌ Difficult | ✅ Built-in identity management |
| Costs | ❌ Variable gas fees | ✅ Fixed operational costs |
| Nigerian legal framework | ❌ Unclear status | ✅ Auditable, controllable |

---

## 2.0 Network Architecture

|-------------|------|---------------|

## 3.0 Chaincode (Smart Contract)

### 3.1 Evidence Chaincode

```go
// chaincode/evidence/evidence.go
package main

import (
    "encoding/json"
    "fmt"
    "time"
    
    "github.com/hyperledger/fabric-contract-api-go/contractapi"
)

// EvidenceChaincode manages the immutable evidence log
type EvidenceChaincode struct {
    contractapi.Contract
}

// =============================================
// DATA STRUCTURES
// =============================================

type AlertRecord struct {
    AlertID       string    `json:"alertId"`
    Timestamp     time.Time `json:"timestamp"`
    LocationHash  string    `json:"locationHash"`  // Hashed location (privacy)
    EvidenceHash  string    `json:"evidenceHash"`  // SHA-256 of evidence file
    EvidenceURI   string    `json:"evidenceUri"`   // IPFS content address
    AlertType     string    `json:"alertType"`     // "emergency", "sentinel", "test"
    Status        string    `json:"status"`        // "active", "acknowledged", "resolved"
    GuardianCount int       `json:"guardianCount"`
    AnomalyScore  float64   `json:"anomalyScore"`
}

type EvidenceEntry struct {
    EntryID      string    `json:"entryId"`
    AlertID      string    `json:"alertId"`
    EvidenceType string    `json:"evidenceType"` // "audio", "video", "location_log"
    FileHash     string    `json:"fileHash"`     // SHA-256 of file
    FileURI      string    `json:"fileUri"`      // IPFS address
    FileSize     int64     `json:"fileSize"`
    Duration     int       `json:"duration"`     // For audio/video
    Timestamp    time.Time `json:"timestamp"`
    UploadedBy   string    `json:"uploadedBy"`   // Device ID
}

type CustodyTransfer struct {
    TransferID  string    `json:"transferId"`
    EvidenceID  string    `json:"evidenceId"`
    FromOrg     string    `json:"fromOrg"`
    ToOrg       string    `json:"toOrg"`
    Reason      string    `json:"reason"`
    Timestamp   time.Time `json:"timestamp"`
    ApprovedBy  string    `json:"approvedBy"`
    AccessLevel string    `json:"accessLevel"` // "view", "download", "share"
}

type AuditLogEntry struct {
    EntryID    string    `json:"entryId"`
    Action     string    `json:"action"`
    PerformedBy string   `json:"performedBy"`
    ResourceID string    `json:"resourceId"`
    Timestamp  time.Time `json:"timestamp"`
    Details    string    `json:"details"`
}

// =============================================
// ALERT RECORDING
// =============================================

// RecordAlert creates an immutable alert record on the ledger
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) RecordAlert(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface, 
    alertJSON string) error {
    
    var alert AlertRecord
    if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(alertJSON), &alert); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("invalid alert data: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if alert.AlertID == "" {
        return fmt.Errorf("alert ID is required")
    }
    if alert.EvidenceHash == "" {
        return fmt.Errorf("evidence hash is required")
    }
    
    // Check for duplicate
    existing, err := ctx.GetStub().GetState(alert.AlertID)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to check for duplicate: %v", err)
    }
    if existing != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("alert %s already exists", alert.AlertID)
    }
    
    // Store alert record
    alertBytes, err := json.Marshal(alert)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal alert: %v", err)
    }
    
    if err := ctx.GetStub().PutState(alert.AlertID, alertBytes); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to store alert: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Emit event for subscribers
    ctx.GetStub().SetEvent("AlertRecorded", alertBytes)
    
    // Log audit entry
    return s.logAudit(ctx, "RECORD_ALERT", alert.AlertID, 
        fmt.Sprintf("Alert %s recorded with hash %s", alert.AlertID, alert.EvidenceHash))
}

// =============================================
// EVIDENCE MANAGEMENT
// =============================================

// AddEvidence adds an evidence entry to an existing alert
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) AddEvidence(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    evidenceJSON string) error {
    
    var evidence EvidenceEntry
    if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(evidenceJSON), &evidence); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("invalid evidence data: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Verify alert exists
    alertBytes, err := ctx.GetStub().GetState(evidence.AlertID)
    if err != nil || alertBytes == nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("alert %s not found", evidence.AlertID)
    }
    
    // Store evidence entry
    evidenceKey := fmt.Sprintf("EVIDENCE_%s", evidence.EntryID)
    evidenceBytes, _ := json.Marshal(evidence)
    
    if err := ctx.GetStub().PutState(evidenceKey, evidenceBytes); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to store evidence: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Create composite key for querying
    compositeKey, _ := ctx.GetStub().CreateCompositeKey("alert-evidence", 
        []string{evidence.AlertID, evidence.EntryID})
    ctx.GetStub().PutState(compositeKey, []byte{0})
    
    return s.logAudit(ctx, "ADD_EVIDENCE", evidence.EntryID,
        fmt.Sprintf("Evidence %s added to alert %s", evidence.EntryID, evidence.AlertID))
}

// =============================================
// CUSTODY CHAIN
// =============================================

// TransferCustody records a chain-of-custody transfer
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) TransferCustody(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    transferJSON string) error {
    
    var transfer CustodyTransfer
    if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(transferJSON), &transfer); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("invalid transfer data: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Verify requester's organization
    clientID, _ := ctx.GetClientIdentity().GetMSPID()
    if clientID != transfer.FromOrg {
        return fmt.Errorf("transfer must be initiated by current custodian")
    }
    
    // Store transfer record
    transferKey := fmt.Sprintf("TRANSFER_%s", transfer.TransferID)
    transferBytes, _ := json.Marshal(transfer)
    
    if err := ctx.GetStub().PutState(transferKey, transferBytes); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("failed to store transfer: %v", err)
    }
    
    // Update evidence custody chain
    custodyKey := fmt.Sprintf("CUSTODY_%s", transfer.EvidenceID)
    ctx.GetStub().PutState(custodyKey, transferBytes)
    
    return s.logAudit(ctx, "TRANSFER_CUSTODY", transfer.EvidenceID,
        fmt.Sprintf("Custody transferred from %s to %s", transfer.FromOrg, transfer.ToOrg))
}

// =============================================
// QUERIES
// =============================================

// GetAlert retrieves an alert record
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) GetAlert(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    alertID string) (*AlertRecord, error) {
    
    alertBytes, err := ctx.GetStub().GetState(alertID)
    if err != nil || alertBytes == nil {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("alert %s not found", alertID)
    }
    
    var alert AlertRecord
    json.Unmarshal(alertBytes, &alert)
    return &alert, nil
}

// GetAlertEvidence retrieves all evidence for an alert
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) GetAlertEvidence(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    alertID string) ([]EvidenceEntry, error) {
    
    // Query composite keys
    iterator, err := ctx.GetStub().GetStateByPartialCompositeKey("alert-evidence", 
        []string{alertID})
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer iterator.Close()
    
    var evidenceList []EvidenceEntry
    for iterator.HasNext() {
        kv, _ := iterator.Next()
        _, compositeParts, _ := ctx.GetStub().SplitCompositeKey(kv.Key)
        
        evidenceKey := fmt.Sprintf("EVIDENCE_%s", compositeParts[1])
        evidenceBytes, _ := ctx.GetStub().GetState(evidenceKey)
        
        var evidence EvidenceEntry
        json.Unmarshal(evidenceBytes, &evidence)
        evidenceList = append(evidenceList, evidence)
    }
    
    return evidenceList, nil
}

// GetCustodyChain retrieves the custody history for evidence
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) GetCustodyChain(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    evidenceID string) ([]CustodyTransfer, error) {
    
    // Query all transfers for this evidence
    queryString := fmt.Sprintf(`{"selector":{"docType":"custodyTransfer","evidenceId":"%s"}}`, 
        evidenceID)
    
    iterator, err := ctx.GetStub().GetQueryResult(queryString)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer iterator.Close()
    
    var transfers []CustodyTransfer
    for iterator.HasNext() {
        kv, _ := iterator.Next()
        var transfer CustodyTransfer
        json.Unmarshal(kv.Value, &transfer)
        transfers = append(transfers, transfer)
    }
    
    return transfers, nil
}

// GetAuditLog retrieves audit entries for a resource
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) GetAuditLog(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    resourceID string) ([]AuditLogEntry, error) {
    
    queryString := fmt.Sprintf(`{"selector":{"resourceId":"%s"},"sort":[{"timestamp":"asc"}]}`, 
        resourceID)
    
    iterator, err := ctx.GetStub().GetQueryResult(queryString)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer iterator.Close()
    
    var entries []AuditLogEntry
    for iterator.HasNext() {
        kv, _ := iterator.Next()
        var entry AuditLogEntry
        json.Unmarshal(kv.Value, &entry)
        entries = append(entries, entry)
    }
    
    return entries, nil
}

// =============================================
// VERIFICATION
// =============================================

// VerifyEvidence verifies the integrity of evidence
func (s *EvidenceChaincode) VerifyEvidence(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    evidenceID string, providedHash string) (bool, error) {
    
    evidenceKey := fmt.Sprintf("EVIDENCE_%s", evidenceID)
    evidenceBytes, err := ctx.GetStub().GetState(evidenceKey)
    if err != nil || evidenceBytes == nil {
        return false, fmt.Errorf("evidence %s not found", evidenceID)
    }
    
    var evidence EvidenceEntry
    json.Unmarshal(evidenceBytes, &evidence)
    
    return evidence.FileHash == providedHash, nil
}

// =============================================
// AUDIT LOGGING
// =============================================

func (s *EvidenceChaincode) logAudit(ctx contractapi.TransactionContextInterface,
    action string, resourceID string, details string) error {
    
    clientID, _ := ctx.GetClientIdentity().GetID()
    
    entry := AuditLogEntry{
        EntryID:    fmt.Sprintf("AUDIT_%d", time.Now().UnixNano()),
        Action:     action,
        PerformedBy: clientID,
        ResourceID: resourceID,
        Timestamp:  time.Now(),
        Details:    details,
    }
    
    entryBytes, _ := json.Marshal(entry)
    return ctx.GetStub().PutState(entry.EntryID, entryBytes)
}

func main() {
    chaincode, _ := contractapi.NewChaincode(&EvidenceChaincode{})
    chaincode.Start()
}

5.0 API Layer
typescript
// api/pillar.ts
import { Gateway, Wallets } from 'fabric-network';
import * as path from 'path';
import * as fs from 'fs';

export class PillarClient {
  private gateway: Gateway;
  private contract: any;
  
  async connect(org: string) {
    const ccpPath = path.resolve(__dirname, `../connection-${org}.json`);
    const ccp = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(ccpPath, 'utf8'));
    
    const wallet = await Wallets.newFileSystemWallet(`../wallet/${org}`);
    
    this.gateway = new Gateway();
    await this.gateway.connect(ccp, {
      wallet,
      identity: org,
      discovery: { enabled: true, asLocalhost: false },
    });
    
    const network = await this.gateway.getNetwork('pillar-channel');
    this.contract = network.getContract('evidence');
  }
  
  async recordAlert(alert: AlertRecord): Promise<string> {
    const result = await this.contract.submitTransaction(
      'RecordAlert',
      JSON.stringify(alert)
    );
    return result.toString();
  }
  
  async addEvidence(evidence: EvidenceEntry): Promise<string> {
    const result = await this.contract.submitTransaction(
      'AddEvidence',
      JSON.stringify(evidence)
    );
    return result.toString();
  }
  
  async verifyEvidence(evidenceId: string, hash: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const result = await this.contract.evaluateTransaction(
      'VerifyEvidence',
      evidenceId,
      hash
    );
    return result.toString() === 'true';
  }
  
  async getCustodyChain(evidenceId: string): Promise<CustodyTransfer[]> {
    const result = await this.contract.evaluateTransaction(
      'GetCustodyChain',
      evidenceId
    );
    return JSON.parse(result.toString());
  }
  
  async disconnect() {
    this.gateway.disconnect();
  }
}




# 08 - Public Transparency Portal

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0 Production
- **Platform:** Web (Next.js), Mobile Web, PWA
- **Users:** General Public, Media, Civil Society, Researchers
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Overview

The Public Portal is the citizen-facing transparency platform. It provides real-time security information without compromising ongoing operations or individual privacy. It serves as both a public good and a deterrent mechanism—showing kidnappers that the environment is monitored and transparent.

### 1.1 Design Philosophy

| Principle | Implementation |
|-----------|----------------|
| **Radical Transparency** | All system metrics publicly visible in real-time |
| **Privacy-Preserving** | No individual data ever exposed; aggregation minimum 50 data points |
| **Actionable Information** | Citizens can make informed safety decisions |
| **Accessible** | Works on 2G connections, low-end devices, screen readers |
| **Deterrent Effect** | Makes criminal operations visible without compromising responses |
| **Trust Building** | Independent verification of system integrity |

---

### 2.2 Risk Heatmap Interaction

```typescript
// components/public/RiskHeatmap.tsx
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import maplibregl from 'maplibre-gl';
import { usePublicData } from '@/hooks/usePublicData';
import { RiskLegend } from './RiskLegend';
import { TimeSlider } from './TimeSlider';
import { LocationSearch } from './LocationSearch';

interface RiskHeatmapProps {
  initialCenter: [number, number];
  initialZoom: number;
}

export const RiskHeatmap: React.FC<RiskHeatmapProps> = ({
  initialCenter = [8.6753, 9.0820], // Nigeria center
  initialZoom = 6,
}) => {
  const [mapLoaded, setMapLoaded] = useState(false);
  const { riskData, alerts, safeZones, isLoading } = usePublicData();
  const mapRef = useRef<maplibregl.Map | null>(null);
  const mapContainerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  
  // Initialize map
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapContainerRef.current || mapRef.current) return;
    
    mapRef.current = new maplibregl.Map({
      container: mapContainerRef.current,
      style: 'https://tiles.aegis.ng/styles/public/style.json',
      center: initialCenter,
      zoom: initialZoom,
      minZoom: 5,
      maxZoom: 18,
    });
    
    mapRef.current.addControl(new maplibregl.NavigationControl(), 'top-right');
    mapRef.current.addControl(new maplibregl.ScaleControl(), 'bottom-left');
    
    mapRef.current.on('load', () => {
      setMapLoaded(true);
    });
    
    return () => {
      mapRef.current?.remove();
    };
  }, []);
  
  // Update risk heatmap layer
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapRef.current || !mapLoaded || !riskData) return;
    
    const source = mapRef.current.getSource('risk-heatmap') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource;
    
    if (!source) {
      mapRef.current.addSource('risk-heatmap', {
        type: 'geojson',
        data: {
          type: 'FeatureCollection',
          features: riskData.features,
        },
      });
      
      mapRef.current.addLayer({
        id: 'risk-heatmap-fill',
        type: 'fill',
        source: 'risk-heatmap',
        paint: {
          'fill-color': [
            'interpolate',
            ['linear'],
            ['get', 'riskScore'],
            0.0, '#00C853',
            0.25, '#FFD600',
            0.5, '#FF9100',
            0.75, '#FF3D00',
            1.0, '#D50000',
          ],
          'fill-opacity': [
            'interpolate',
            ['linear'],
            ['zoom'],
            5, 0.15,
            10, 0.25,
            15, 0.35,
          ],
        },
      });
    } else {
      source.setData({
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: riskData.features,
      });
    }
  }, [riskData, mapLoaded]);
  
  // Update safe zones
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapRef.current || !mapLoaded || !safeZones) return;
    
    const source = mapRef.current.getSource('safe-zones') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource;
    
    if (!source) {
      mapRef.current.addSource('safe-zones', {
        type: 'geojson',
        data: {
          type: 'FeatureCollection',
          features: safeZones.features,
        },
      });
      
      mapRef.current.addLayer({
        id: 'safe-zones-markers',
        type: 'circle',
        source: 'safe-zones',
        paint: {
          'circle-radius': 8,
          'circle-color': '#4CAF50',
          'circle-stroke-width': 2,
          'circle-stroke-color': '#FFFFFF',
        },
      });
      
      // Add click handler
      mapRef.current.on('click', 'safe-zones-markers', (e) => {
        if (e.features?.[0]) {
          showSafeZonePopup(e.features[0], e.lngLat);
        }
      });
    } else {
      source.setData({
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: safeZones.features,
      });
    }
  }, [safeZones, mapLoaded]);
  
  // Update alert clusters (anonymized, delayed)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapRef.current || !mapLoaded || !alerts) return;
    
    const source = mapRef.current.getSource('alert-clusters') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource;
    
    if (!source) {
      mapRef.current.addSource('alert-clusters', {
        type: 'geojson',
        data: {
          type: 'FeatureCollection',
          features: alerts.clusters,
        },
        cluster: true,
        clusterMaxZoom: 12,
        clusterRadius: 50,
      });
      
      mapRef.current.addLayer({
        id: 'alert-clusters',
        type: 'circle',
        source: 'alert-clusters',
        filter: ['has', 'point_count'],
        paint: {
          'circle-color': [
            'step',
            ['get', 'point_count'],
            '#FFD600',
            10,
            '#FF9100',
            50,
            '#FF3D00',
            100,
            '#D50000',
          ],
          'circle-radius': [
            'step',
            ['get', 'point_count'],
            20,
            10,
            30,
            50,
            40,
          ],
          'circle-opacity': 0.6,
        },
      });
      
      mapRef.current.addLayer({
        id: 'alert-cluster-count',
        type: 'symbol',
        source: 'alert-clusters',
        filter: ['has', 'point_count'],
        layout: {
          'text-field': '{point_count_abbreviated}',
          'text-font': ['Inter Bold'],
          'text-size': 12,
        },
        paint: {
          'text-color': '#FFFFFF',
        },
      });
    } else {
      source.setData({
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: alerts.clusters,
      });
    }
  }, [alerts, mapLoaded]);
  
  return (
    <div className="relative w-full h-[60vh] min-h-[400px] rounded-lg overflow-hidden shadow-xl">
      <div ref={mapContainerRef} className="w-full h-full" />
      
      {/* Overlay Controls */}
      <div className="absolute top-4 left-4 space-y-2 z-10">
        <RiskLegend />
      </div>
      
      <div className="absolute top-4 right-4 z-10">
        <LocationSearch onSelect={flyToLocation} />
      </div>
      
      <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-4 right-4 z-10">
        <TimeSlider onChange={updateTimeFilter} />
      </div>
      
      {/* Loading Overlay */}
      {isLoading && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/10 flex items-center justify-center">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg px-6 py-3 shadow-lg">
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
              <Spinner />
              <span>Updating safety data...</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {/* Update Timestamp */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-4 right-4 bg-white/90 rounded px-3 py-1 text-xs">
        Updated: {riskData?.timestamp || 'Loading...'}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

function showSafeZonePopup(feature: GeoJSON.Feature, lngLat: maplibregl.LngLat) {
  const props = feature.properties;
  const popup = new maplibregl.Popup({ offset: 15 })
    .setLngLat(lngLat)
    .setHTML(`
      <div style="padding: 8px;">
        <strong>${props.name}</strong><br/>
        <span style="font-size: 12px; color: #666;">${props.type}</span><br/>
        <span style="font-size: 12px;">📞 ${props.phone || 'N/A'}</span><br/>
        <span style="font-size: 12px;">🕐 ${props.hours || '24/7'}</span>
      </div>
    `)
    .addTo(mapRef.current!);
}
2.3 Community Reporting Interface
typescript
// components/public/CommunityReport.tsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { useSubmitReport } from '@/hooks/useSubmitReport';

const reportSchema = z.object({
  location: z.object({
    latitude: z.number(),
    longitude: z.number(),
  }),
  category: z.enum([
    'suspicious_activity',
    'checkpoint',
    'road_condition',
    'safe_passage',
    'incident_witness',
    'other',
  ]),
  description: z.string().min(10).max(500),
  timestamp: z.date(),
  isAnonymous: z.boolean(),
  contactPhone: z.string().optional(),
});

type ReportForm = z.infer<typeof reportSchema>;

export const CommunityReportForm: React.FC = () => {
  const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [isSubmitted, setIsSubmitted] = useState(false);
  const [selectedLocation, setSelectedLocation] = useState<[number, number] | null>(null);
  
  const { register, handleSubmit, setValue, formState: { errors } } = useForm<ReportForm>({
    resolver: zodResolver(reportSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      isAnonymous: true,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    },
  });
  
  const submitReport = useSubmitReport();
  
  const onSubmit = async (data: ReportForm) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    try {
      await submitReport(data);
      setIsSubmitted(true);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to submit report:', error);
    } finally {
      setIsSubmitting(false);
    }
  };
  
  if (isSubmitted) {
    return (
      <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-6 text-center">
        <div className="text-4xl mb-3">✅</div>
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-green-800">Report Submitted</h3>
        <p className="text-green-600 mt-2">
          Thank you for helping keep your community safe. 
          Your report will be verified and may appear on the map within 15 minutes.
        </p>
        <button
          onClick={() => setIsSubmitted(false)}
          className="mt-4 text-green-700 underline"
        >
          Submit Another Report
        </button>
      </div>
    );
  }
  
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Report a Safety Observation</h3>
      
      {/* Category Selection */}
      <div>
        <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-2">What did you observe?</label>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
          {[
            { value: 'suspicious_activity', label: '🕵️ Suspicious Activity', icon: '🔍' },
            { value: 'checkpoint', label: '🛑 Checkpoint', icon: '🚧' },
            { value: 'road_condition', label: '🛣️ Road Condition', icon: '🛤️' },
            { value: 'safe_passage', label: '✅ Safe Passage', icon: '🟢' },
            { value: 'incident_witness', label: '⚠️ Incident', icon: '🚨' },
            { value: 'other', label: '📝 Other', icon: '💬' },
          ].map((option) => (
            <button
              key={option.value}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setValue('category', option.value as any)}
              className={`p-3 rounded-lg border text-left text-sm transition-all ${
                errors.category ? 'border-red-300' : 'border-gray-200'
              } hover:border-green-400 hover:bg-green-50`}
            >
              <span className="mr-2">{option.icon}</span>
              {option.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
        {errors.category && (
          <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">Please select a category</p>
        )}
      </div>
      
      {/* Location Picker */}
      <div>
        <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-2">Where did this happen?</label>
        <div className="h-40 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer"
             onClick={openLocationPicker}>
          {selectedLocation ? (
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-2xl">📍</div>
              <p className="text-sm mt-1">
                {selectedLocation[0].toFixed(4)}, {selectedLocation[1].toFixed(4)}
              </p>
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Tap to change</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="text-center text-gray-500">
              <div className="text-2xl">🗺️</div>
              <p>Tap to select location on map</p>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Description */}
      <div>
        <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-2">Description</label>
        <textarea
          {...register('description')}
          rows={4}
          className={`w-full p-3 border rounded-lg ${
            errors.description ? 'border-red-300' : 'border-gray-200'
          }`}
          placeholder="Describe what you observed. Include relevant details but do NOT share personal information about others."
          maxLength={500}
        />
        <div className="flex justify-between mt-1">
          {errors.description && (
            <p className="text-red-500 text-xs">{errors.description.message}</p>
          )}
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">Maximum 500 characters</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Time */}
      <div>
        <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-2">When did this happen?</label>
        <input
          type="datetime-local"
          {...register('timestamp', { valueAsDate: true })}
          className="w-full p-3 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg"
        />
      </div>
      
      {/* Anonymous Toggle */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg">
        <div>
          <p className="font-medium">Submit Anonymously</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Your identity will not be shared</p>
        </div>
        <label className="relative inline-flex items-center cursor-pointer">
          <input
            type="checkbox"
            {...register('isAnonymous')}
            className="sr-only peer"
          />
          <div className="w-11 h-6 bg-gray-200 peer-focus:ring-2 peer-focus:ring-green-300 
                          rounded-full peer peer-checked:after:translate-x-full 
                          peer-checked:bg-green-600 after:content-[''] after:absolute 
                          after:top-[2px] after:left-[2px] after:bg-white after:rounded-full 
                          after:h-5 after:w-5 after:transition-all">
          </div>
        </label>
      </div>
      
      {/* Contact (if not anonymous) */}
      {!register('isAnonymous') && (
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-2">
            Contact Phone (for verification only)
          </label>
          <input
            type="tel"
            {...register('contactPhone')}
            className="w-full p-3 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg"
            placeholder="+234 800 000 0000"
          />
        </div>
      )}
      
      {/* Submit */}
      <button
        type="submit"
        disabled={isSubmitting}
        className="w-full py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-lg font-semibold
                   hover:bg-green-700 disabled:bg-gray-400 transition-colors"
      >
        {isSubmitting ? 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Report'}
      </button>
      
      {/* Disclaimer */}
      <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 text-center">
        By submitting, you confirm this information is true to the best of your knowledge.
        False reports may be flagged and removed. Your submission helps keep communities safe.
      </p>
    </form>
  );
};

6.0 Technical Implementation
6.1 Public API
typescript
// pages/api/public/risk-data.ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { getPublicRiskData } from '@/lib/public-data';
import { rateLimiter } from '@/lib/rate-limiter';
import { cacheControl } from '@/lib/cache';

export default async function handler(
  req: NextApiRequest,
  res: NextApiResponse
) {
  // Rate limiting (prevent abuse while allowing public access)
  const limiter = rateLimiter({
    interval: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
    uniqueTokenPerInterval: 500,
  });
  
  try {
    await limiter.check(res, 60, 'PUBLIC_RISK_DATA'); // 60 requests per minute
  } catch {
    return res.status(429).json({ error: 'Rate limit exceeded. Please try again shortly.' });
  }
  
  // Cache control (data updates every 60 seconds)
  cacheControl(res, {
    public: true,
    maxAge: 60,
    staleWhileRevalidate: 120,
  });
  
  try {
    const data = await getPublicRiskData();
    res.status(200).json(data);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to fetch public risk data:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error' });
  }
}

// next.config.js (public portal specific)
module.exports = {
  async headers() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/:path*',
        headers: [
          {
            key: 'Content-Security-Policy',
            value: [
              "default-src 'self'",
              "script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://tiles.aegis.ng",
              "style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'",
              "img-src 'self' data: https://tiles.aegis.ng https://cdn.aegis.ng",
              "connect-src 'self' https://api.aegis.ng wss://api.aegis.ng",
              "font-src 'self'",
              "frame-src 'none'",
              "object-src 'none'",
            ].join('; '),
          },
          {
            key: 'X-Frame-Options',
            value: 'DENY',
          },
          {
            key: 'X-Content-Type-Options',
            value: 'nosniff',
          },
          {
            key: 'Referrer-Policy',
            value: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin',
          },
        ],
      },
    ];
  },
};



# 09 - Complete API Reference

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Base URL:** `https://api.aegis.ng/v2`
- **WebSocket:** `wss://api.aegis.ng/ws`
- **Authentication:** Bearer JWT + API Key
- **Content Type:** application/json
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Authentication

### 1.1 Device Registration

```http

8.0 WebSocket Streams
8.1 Alert Stream (Command Center)
javascript
const ws = new WebSocket('wss://api.aegis.ng/ws/command/alerts');
ws.send(JSON.stringify({
  type: 'auth',
  token: 'eyJhbGciOiJFUzI1NiIs...',
  region: 'north-central'
}));

// Incoming messages
ws.onmessage = (event) => {
  const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
  
  switch(data.type) {
    case 'alert_new':
      // New emergency alert
      console.log('New alert:', data.alert);
      break;
    case 'alert_update':
      // Alert status update
      console.log('Alert updated:', data.alert_id, data.changes);
      break;
    case 'unit_location':
      // Responding unit location update
      console.log('Unit moved:', data.unit_id, data.location);
      break;
    case 'guardian_response':
      // Guardian acknowledged alert
      console.log('Guardian responded:', data.guardian_name);
      break;
  }
};
8.2 Location Stream (Guardian)
javascript
const ws = new WebSocket(`wss://api.aegis.ng/ws/guardian/track/${alertId}`);
ws.send(JSON.stringify({
  type: 'auth',
  token: guardianToken
}));

ws.onmessage = (event) => {
  const location = JSON.parse(event.data);
  updateMapMarker(location.latitude, location.longitude);
  updateSpeedIndicator(location.speed);
  updateHeading(location.heading);
};
9.0 Error Codes
Code	Description	Resolution
AUTH_001	Invalid credentials	Re-authenticate
AUTH_002	Token expired	Refresh token
AUTH_003	Insufficient permissions	Request access upgrade
ALERT_001	Duplicate alert	Ignore, alert already active
ALERT_002	Alert not found	Verify alert ID
ALERT_003	Alert already resolved	No action needed
SENTINEL_001	Session limit reached	End existing session first
SENTINEL_002	Insufficient capabilities	Enable required sensors
RATE_001	Rate limit exceeded	Implement exponential backoff
SERVER_001	Internal server error	Retry with exponential backoff
SERVER_002	Service temporarily unavailable	Retry after Retry-After header
9.1 Rate Limits
Endpoint Group	Limit	Window
Alert triggers	10	Per minute
Alert status checks	60	Per minute
Scan uploads	12	Per minute
Location updates	120	Per minute
Public API	60	Per minute per IP
Guardian API	300	Per minute
10.0 SDK Examples
10.1 Flutter/Dart
dart
import 'package:aegis_sdk/aegis_sdk.dart';

final aegis = AegisClient(
  apiKey: 'aegis_sk_xxxxxxxx',
  deviceId: 'DEV-2024-XXXXX',
);

// Trigger emergency
final alert = await aegis.triggerEmergency(
  location: Location(10.5234, 7.4356),
  triggerMethod: TriggerMethod.buttonHold,
);

// Start Sentinel Mode
final session = await aegis.startSentinelSession(
  location: Location(10.5234, 7.4356),
);

// Upload scan
await aegis.submitScan(ScanData(
  sessionId: session.id,
  devices: scannedDevices,
  location: Location(10.5234, 7.4356),
));
10.2 JavaScript/TypeScript
typescript
import { AegisClient } from '@aegis/sdk';

const aegis = new AegisClient({
  apiKey: 'aegis_sk_xxxxxxxx',
  deviceId: 'DEV-2024-XXXXX',
});

// Trigger emergency
const alert = await aegis.triggerEmergency({
  location: { latitude: 10.5234, longitude: 7.4356 },
  triggerMethod: 'button_hold',
});

// Stream location updates (Guardian)
const stream = aegis.streamVictimLocation(alert.alertId);
stream.on('location', (location) => {
  console.log('Victim at:', location);
});
End of API Reference Complete Documentation




# 10 - Complete Database Schema

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Databases:** Neo4j (Graph), PostgreSQL (Relational), Redis (Cache), TimescaleDB (Time-Series)
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Neo4j Graph Database

### 1.1 Node Labels

```cypher
// =============================================

1.2 Relationships
cypher
// =============================================
// USER RELATIONSHIPS
// =============================================

// User trusts Guardian
(:User)-[:TRUSTS {
  since: datetime('2026-06-01T00:00:00Z'),
  relationship: 'family',
  is_primary: true,
  notification_priority: 1
}]->(:Guardian)

// Guardian responds to Alert
(:Guardian)-[:ACKNOWLEDGED {
  timestamp: datetime('2026-06-10T14:33:45Z'),
  response_time_seconds: 90,
  message: 'I am mobilizing family members.'
}]->(:Alert)

// =============================================
// ALERT RELATIONSHIPS
// =============================================

// User triggered Alert
(:User)-[:TRIGGERED {
  timestamp: datetime('2026-06-10T14:32:15Z'),
  sequence_number: 42}]->(:Alert)

// Alert occurred in GridCell
(:Alert)-[:OCCURRED_IN]->(:GridCell)

// Alert has LocationPoints
(:Alert)-[:HAS_LOCATION {
  order: 1
}]->(:LocationPoint)

// LocationPoints form a track
(:LocationPoint)-[:NEXT]->(:LocationPoint)

// Alert has Evidence
(:Alert)-[:HAS_EVIDENCE]->(:Evidence)

// =============================================
// DEVICE RELATIONSHIPS
// =============================================

// Device detected at GridCell
(:Device)-[:DETECTED_AT {
  timestamp: datetime('2026-06-10T14:32:00Z'),
  rssi: -65,
  session_id: 'SES-20240610-1430-XXXX'
}]->(:GridCell)

// Devices co-occur (materialized for performance)
(:Device)-[:CO_OCCURS_WITH {
  count: 15,
  last_seen_together: datetime('2026-06-10T14:32:00Z'),
  locations: ['GRID-1052-7435', 'GRID-1052-7436']
}]->(:Device)

// =============================================
// SAFE ZONE RELATIONSHIPS
// =============================================

(:SafeZone)-[:LOCATED_IN]->(:GridCell)

// =============================================
// INDEXES
// =============================================

CREATE INDEX user_uuid IF NOT EXISTS FOR (u:User) ON (u.uuid);
CREATE INDEX guardian_uuid IF NOT EXISTS FOR (g:Guardian) ON (g.uuid);
CREATE INDEX alert_id IF NOT EXISTS FOR (a:Alert) ON (a.id);
CREATE INDEX grid_cell_id IF NOT EXISTS FOR (g:GridCell) ON (g.id);
CREATE INDEX device_mac_hash IF NOT EXISTS FOR (d:Device) ON (d.mac_hash);
CREATE INDEX location_timestamp IF NOT EXISTS FOR (l:LocationPoint) ON (l.timestamp);
CREATE INDEX alert_timestamp IF NOT EXISTS FOR (a:Alert) ON (a.timestamp);
CREATE INDEX alert_status IF NOT EXISTS FOR (a:Alert) ON (a.status);

// Spatial index for location queries
CREATE POINT INDEX location_point IF NOT EXISTS FOR (l:LocationPoint) ON (l.location);
1.3 Key Cypher Queries
cypher
// =============================================
// FIND ACTIVE ALERTS IN REGION
// =============================================
MATCH (a:Alert {status: 'active'})-[:OCCURRED_IN]->(gc:GridCell)
WHERE gc.id STARTS WITH 'GRID-10'
RETURN a.id, a.timestamp, a.priority, gc.centroid_lat, gc.centroid_lng
ORDER BY a.priority DESC, a.timestamp DESC;

// =============================================
// FIND GUARDIANS FOR ALERT
// =============================================
MATCH (u:User)-[:TRIGGERED]->(a:Alert {id: $alertId})
MATCH (u)-[:TRUSTS]->(g:Guardian)
RETURN g.display_name, g.phone_hash, g.average_response_time_seconds;

// =============================================
// FIND SUSPICIOUS DEVICE CLUSTERS
// =============================================
MATCH (d1:Device)-[:CO_OCCURS_WITH]-(d2:Device)
WHERE d1.suspicious_score > 0.5 AND d2.suspicious_score > 0.5
  AND d1 <> d2
WITH d1, d2, 
     [(d1)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc:GridCell) | gc.id] AS d1_locations,
     [(d2)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc:GridCell) | gc.id] AS d2_locations
WHERE size([loc IN d1_locations WHERE loc IN d2_locations]) >= 3
RETURN d1.mac_hash, d2.mac_hash, 
       [loc IN d1_locations WHERE loc IN d2_locations] AS common_locations
ORDER BY size(common_locations) DESC;

// =============================================
// CALCULATE GRID CELL RISK
// =============================================
MATCH (gc:GridCell {id: $gridId})
OPTIONAL MATCH (a:Alert)-[:OCCURRED_IN]->(gc)
  WHERE a.timestamp > datetime() - duration('P90D')
WITH gc, count(a) AS recent_incidents
OPTIONAL MATCH (d:Device)-[:DETECTED_AT]->(gc)
  WHERE d.last_seen > datetime() - duration('PT1H')
WITH gc, recent_incidents, count(d) AS current_devices
SET gc.risk_score = 
  (recent_incidents * 0.3 / 10.0) +
  (CASE WHEN current_devices > gc.average_device_count * 2 
        THEN 0.4 ELSE current_devices * 0.1 / gc.average_device_count END)
RETURN gc.id, gc.risk_score;

// =============================================
// TRACE VICTIM MOVEMENT
// =============================================
MATCH (a:Alert {id: $alertId})-[:HAS_LOCATION]->(lp:LocationPoint)
RETURN lp.location.latitude AS lat, 
       lp.location.longitude AS lng,
       lp.timestamp AS ts,
       lp.speed,
       lp.heading
ORDER BY lp.timestamp;

-- =============================================
-- USERS TABLE

CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    phone_hash VARCHAR(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    display_name VARCHAR(100),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    last_active TIMESTAMPTZ,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    trust_score DECIMAL(3,2) DEFAULT 0.50,
    total_alerts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    false_alarms INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    device_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    preferred_language VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en',
    notification_preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{"push": true, "sms": true}',
    encrypted_pii BYTEA, -- Encrypted PII, requires court order + key
    pii_access_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    pii_last_accessed TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- =============================================
-- DEVICES TABLE
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE devices (
    id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    platform VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, -- 'android' or 'ios'
    platform_version VARCHAR(20),
    app_version VARCHAR(10),
    device_model VARCHAR(100),
    public_key TEXT NOT NULL,
    api_key_hash VARCHAR(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    push_token VARCHAR(255),
    lora_capable BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    last_active TIMESTAMPTZ,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE
);

-- =============================================
-- GUARDIANS TABLE
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE guardians (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    phone_hash VARCHAR(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    display_name VARCHAR(100),
    email_hash VARCHAR(64),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    last_active TIMESTAMPTZ,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    total_acknowledgments INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    average_response_time_seconds DECIMAL(7,2),
    reliability_score DECIMAL(3,2) DEFAULT 0.50,
    push_token VARCHAR(255),
    notification_preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{"push": true, "sms": true, "email": false}'
);

-- USER-GUARDIAN RELATIONSHIPS
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE user_guardians (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    guardian_id UUID REFERENCES guardians(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    relationship VARCHAR(50), -- 'family', 'friend', 'colleague'
    is_primary BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    notification_priority INTEGER DEFAULT 2,
    added_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    UNIQUE(user_id, guardian_id)
);

-- =============================================
-- ALERTS TABLE
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE alerts (
    id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    device_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES devices(id),
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active', -- 'active', 'acknowledged', 'resolved', 'cancelled'
    priority VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'high', -- 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
    trigger_method VARCHAR(30),
    triggered_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    cancelled_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    initial_lat DECIMAL(10,7),
    initial_lng DECIMAL(10,7),
    battery_level INTEGER,
    network_type VARCHAR(10),
    signal_strength INTEGER,
    is_silent BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    anomaly_score DECIMAL(4,3),
    resolution_type VARCHAR(50),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

    accuracy DECIMAL(7,2),
    altitude DECIMAL(7,2),
    speed DECIMAL(7,2),
    heading DECIMAL(6,2),

    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

# =============================================
# KEY PATTERNS
# =============================================

# Active alerts (Hash)
alert:{alert_id}
  - status: "active"
  - priority: "critical"
  - lat: "10.5234"
  - lng: "7.4356"
  - triggered_at: "2026-06-10T14:32:15Z"
  - guardians_acknowledged: "2"
  - last_update: "2026-06-10T14:35:00Z"
  TTL: 3600 (1 hour after resolution)

# Active alerts index (Sorted Set)
active_alerts:{region}
  Members: alert_ids
  Scores: timestamp (for ordering)
  TTL: N/A (maintained in real-time)

# Device session (Hash)
device:{device_id}
  - user_id: "USR-2024-XXXXX"
  - platform: "android"
  - push_token: "xxx"
  - last_active: "2026-06-10T14:30:00Z"
  - current_session: "SES-20240610-1430-XXXX"
  - sentinel_active: "true"
  TTL: 86400 (24 hours)

# Location cache (String - JSON)
location:{device_id}
  Value: {"lat":10.5234,"lng":7.4356,"accuracy":5.0,"speed":45.0,"heading":278.0,"ts":"2026-06-10T14:35:00Z"}
  TTL: 30 (30 seconds)

# Risk score cache (String)
risk:{grid_id}
  Value: "0.62"
  TTL: 60 (60 seconds)

# Rate limiting (String)
ratelimit:{endpoint}:{identifier}
  Value: count
  TTL: window_seconds

# Guardian response cache (Set)
guardian_responses:{alert_id}
  Members: guardian_ids that have acknowledged
  TTL: 3600

# SMS verification codes (String)
sms_verify:{phone_hash}
  Value: "123456"
  TTL: 300 (5 minutes)

# WebSocket connections (Hash)
ws:{user_id}
  - connection_id: "xxx"
  - connected_at: "2026-06-10T14:30:00Z"
  - server: "ws-01"
  TTL: 86400

# Public data cache (String - JSON)
public:risk_map:{bounds_hash}
  Value: { ... risk map data ... }
  TTL: 60

public:statistics
  Value: { ... system statistics ... }
  TTL: 60

# 11 - Security Protocol & Encryption Specification

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Classification:** Confidential
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10

---

## 1.0 Encryption Standards

### 1.1 Data at Rest

| Data Type | Algorithm | Key Size | Mode | Key Management |
|-----------|-----------|----------|------|----------------|
| User PII | AES-256 | 256-bit | GCM | AWS KMS / HashiCorp Vault |
| Alert data | AES-256 | 256-bit | GCM | Per-alert derived key |
| Audio recordings | AES-256 | 256-bit | GCM | Per-chunk unique key |
| Location history | AES-256 | 256-bit | GCM | User-specific key |
| Device scans | AES-256 | 256-bit | CBC | Session-specific key |
| Database backups | AES-256 | 256-bit | GCM | Master backup key |

### 1.2 Data in Transit

| Channel | Protocol | Encryption | Key Exchange |
|---------|----------|------------|--------------|
| App ↔ API | TLS 1.3 | AES-256-GCM | ECDHE with P-256 |
| API ↔ Database | TLS 1.3 | AES-256-GCM | ECDHE with P-256 |
| LoRa Mesh | AES-256-CBC | Pre-shared key | Provisioned at deployment |
| SMS Fallback | AES-256-GCM | Pre-shared key | Derived from guardian relationship |
| WebSocket | TLS 1.3 | AES-256-GCM | ECDHE with P-256 |
| Inter-service (Kafka) | TLS 1.3 | AES-256-GCM | Mutual TLS |

### 1.3 Key Hierarchy
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ ROOT KEY (HSM) │
│ Stored in AWS CloudHSM / YubiHSM │
└───────────────┬─────────────────────────────┬───────────────────┘
│ │
┌───────────▼───────────┐ ┌───────────▼───────────┐
│ MASTER DATA KEY │ │ MASTER COMM KEY │
│ (Encrypts DB keys) │ │ (Encrypts transport) │
└───────────┬───────────┘ └───────────┬───────────┘
│ │
┌───────────▼───────────┐ ┌───────────▼───────────┐
│ PER-USER KEY │ │ PER-DEVICE KEY │
│ (User data) │ │ (Device auth) │
└───────────┬───────────┘ └───────────┬───────────┘
│ │
┌───────────▼───────────┐ ┌───────────▼───────────┐
│ PER-ALERT KEY │ │ SESSION KEY │
│ (Alert-specific) │ │ (Temporary) │
└───────────────────────┘ └───────────────────────┘

text

---

## 2.0 Encryption Implementation

### 2.1 Alert Encryption (End-to-End)

```python
# alert_encryption.py
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import x25519
import os
import json

class AlertEncryption:
    """
    End-to-end encryption for emergency alerts.
    Ensures only intended guardians can decrypt the alert payload.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, device_private_key, guardian_public_keys):
        self.device_private_key = device_private_key
        self.guardian_public_keys = guardian_public_keys
    
    def encrypt_alert(self, alert_data: dict) -> dict:
        """
        Encrypt alert for multiple guardians.
        Uses hybrid encryption: ECDH for key exchange, AES-GCM for data.
        """
        # Generate ephemeral key pair for this alert
        ephemeral_private = x25519.X25519PrivateKey.generate()
        ephemeral_public = ephemeral_private.public_key()
        
        # Generate data encryption key
        data_key = AESGCM.generate_key(bit_length=256)
        
        # Encrypt alert data with data key
        aesgcm = AESGCM(data_key)
        nonce = os.urandom(12)
        plaintext = json.dumps(alert_data).encode('utf-8')
        ciphertext = aesgcm.encrypt(nonce, plaintext, None)
        
        # Encrypt data key for each guardian
        encrypted_keys = {}
        for guardian_id, guardian_public_key in self.guardian_public_keys.items():
            shared_key = ephemeral_private.exchange(guardian_public_key)
            derived_key = HKDF(
                algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
                length=32,
                salt=None,
                info=b'aegis-alert-key-wrap',
            ).derive(shared_key)
            
            key_wrap_aesgcm = AESGCM(derived_key)
            key_nonce = os.urandom(12)
            encrypted_key = key_wrap_aesgcm.encrypt(key_nonce, data_key, None)
            
            encrypted_keys[guardian_id] = {
                'encrypted_key': encrypted_key.hex(),
                'nonce': key_nonce.hex(),
            }
        
        # Device signature for authenticity
        signature = self._sign_alert(ciphertext)
        
        return {
            'ephemeral_public_key': ephemeral_public.public_bytes_raw().hex(),
            'ciphertext': ciphertext.hex(),
            'nonce': nonce.hex(),
            'encrypted_keys': encrypted_keys,
            'device_signature': signature.hex(),
        }
    
    def decrypt_alert(self, encrypted_alert: dict, guardian_private_key) -> dict:
        """
        Guardian decrypts alert using their private key.
        """
        # Reconstruct ephemeral public key
        ephemeral_public = x25519.X25519PublicKey.from_public_bytes(
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_alert['ephemeral_public_key'])
        )
        
        # Derive shared key
        shared_key = guardian_private_key.exchange(ephemeral_public)
        derived_key = HKDF(
            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
            length=32,
            salt=None,
            info=b'aegis-alert-key-wrap',
        ).derive(shared_key)
        
        # Decrypt data key
        encrypted_key_data = encrypted_alert['encrypted_keys'][guardian_id]
        key_wrap_aesgcm = AESGCM(derived_key)
        data_key = key_wrap_aesgcm.decrypt(
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_key_data['nonce']),
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_key_data['encrypted_key']),
            None
        )
        
        # Decrypt alert data
        aesgcm = AESGCM(data_key)
        plaintext = aesgcm.decrypt(
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_alert['nonce']),
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_alert['ciphertext']),
            None
        )
        
        # Verify device signature
        if not self._verify_signature(
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_alert['ciphertext']),
            bytes.fromhex(encrypted_alert['device_signature'])
        ):
            raise SecurityException("Alert signature verification failed")
        
        return json.loads(plaintext.decode('utf-8'))
    
    def _sign_alert(self, ciphertext: bytes) -> bytes:
        """Sign alert with device private key for authenticity."""
        from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import ed25519
        # In production, use Ed25519 for signatures
        return b''  # Placeholder
    
    def _verify_signature(self, ciphertext: bytes, signature: bytes) -> bool:
        """Verify device signature."""
        return True  # Placeholder
2.2 SMS Encryption
python
# sms_encryption.py
import base64
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
import os

class SMSEncryption:
    """
    Encrypts SMS alerts for the fallback channel.
    Must work within 160-character SMS limits.
    """
    
    SMS_MAX_LENGTH = 160
    # Overhead: nonce(12) + tag(16) + metadata = ~40 bytes base64 = ~54 chars
    MAX_PAYLOAD_LENGTH = 106  # characters
    
    def __init__(self, pre_shared_key: bytes):
        if len(pre_shared_key) != 32:
            raise ValueError("Pre-shared key must be 32 bytes")
        self.key = pre_shared_key
    
    def encrypt_location_alert(self, lat: float, lng: float, timestamp: int, 
                               battery: int, device_id: str) -> str:
        """
        Encrypt a minimal location alert for SMS.
        Returns base64 string suitable for SMS.
        """
        aesgcm = AESGCM(self.key)
        nonce = os.urandom(12)
        
        # Compact binary format
        import struct
        payload = struct.pack(
            '!ffII6s',
            lat,           # 4 bytes
            lng,           # 4 bytes
            timestamp,     # 4 bytes
            battery,       # 4 bytes
            device_id.encode()[:6]  # 6 bytes
        )
        
        ciphertext = aesgcm.encrypt(nonce, payload, None)
        
        # Combine nonce + ciphertext (includes tag)
        combined = nonce + ciphertext
        
        # Base64 encode
        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(combined).decode('ascii')
    
    def decrypt_location_alert(self, sms_body: str) -> dict:
        """
        Decrypt SMS alert back to location data.
        """
        aesgcm = AESGCM(self.key)
        
        combined = base64.urlsafe_b64decode(sms_body.encode('ascii'))
        
        nonce = combined[:12]
        ciphertext = combined[12:]
        
        payload = aesgcm.decrypt(nonce, ciphertext, None)
        
        import struct
        lat, lng, timestamp, battery = struct.unpack('!ffII', payload[:16])
        device_id = payload[16:22].decode('ascii').strip()
        
        return {
            'latitude': lat,
            'longitude': lng,
            'timestamp': timestamp,
            'battery': battery,
            'device_id': device_id,
        }
