3.2 Multi-Factor Authentication (Command Center)
python
# mfa.py
import pyotp
from webauthn import verify_authentication_response
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes

class CommandCenterAuth:
    """
    Multi-factor authentication for Command Center access.
    Requires: Password + TOTP + Hardware Security Key
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.totp = pyotp.TOTP('base32secretkey')
        self.failed_attempts = {}  # Rate limiting
    
    async def authenticate(self, username: str, password: str, 
                          totp_code: str, webauthn_response: dict) -> dict:
        """
        Full MFA authentication flow.
        """
        # Rate limiting
        if self._is_rate_limited(username):
            raise AuthenticationError("Too many attempts. Try again in 15 minutes.")
        
        # Step 1: Password verification
        user = await self._verify_password(username, password)
        if not user:
            self._record_failure(username)
            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid credentials")
        
        # Step 2: TOTP verification
        if not self.totp.verify(totp_code):
            self._record_failure(username)
            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid verification code")
        
        # Step 3: Hardware security key (WebAuthn)
        if not await self._verify_webauthn(user, webauthn_response):
            self._record_failure(username)
            raise AuthenticationError("Security key verification failed")
        
        # Step 4: Generate session token
        token = self._generate_session_token(user)
        
        # Step 5: Log successful authentication
        await self._log_auth_event(user, success=True)
        
        return token
    
    def _is_rate_limited(self, username: str) -> bool:
        """Check if user has exceeded rate limit."""
        attempts = self.failed_attempts.get(username, [])
        recent = [t for t in attempts if (datetime.now() - t).seconds < 900]
        return len(recent) >= 5
    
    def _record_failure(self, username: str):
        """Record failed authentication attempt."""
        if username not in self.failed_attempts:
            self.failed_attempts[username] = []
        self.failed_attempts[username].append(datetime.now())
4.0 Privacy Protection
4.1 Differential Privacy Implementation
python
# differential_privacy.py
import numpy as np
from typing import List, Tuple

class DifferentialPrivacy:
    """
    Implements ε-differential privacy for data aggregation.
    Ensures individual contributions cannot be identified.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, epsilon: float = 0.1):
        """
        Args:
            epsilon: Privacy budget (lower = more privacy, more noise)
        """
        self.epsilon = epsilon
    
    def add_laplace_noise(self, value: float, sensitivity: float = 1.0) -> float:
        """
        Add Laplace noise for numeric values.
        """
        scale = sensitivity / self.epsilon
        noise = np.random.laplace(0, scale)
        return value + noise
    
    def randomized_response(self, true_value: bool, p: float = 0.75) -> bool:
        """
        Randomized response for boolean values.
        User answers truthfully with probability p, 
        randomly with probability 1-p.
        """
        if np.random.random() < p:
            return true_value
        else:
            return np.random.random() < 0.5
    
    def anonymize_device_count(self, count: int) -> int:
        """
        Anonymize device scan counts.
        Adds noise and rounds to nearest integer.
        """
        noisy = self.add_laplace_noise(float(count), sensitivity=1.0)
        return max(0, int(round(noisy)))
    
    def anonymize_location(self, lat: float, lng: float, 
                          radius_meters: float = 200) -> Tuple[float, float]:
        """
        Anonymize location by adding random offset within radius.
        """
        # Convert radius to degrees (approximate)
        radius_deg = radius_meters / 111320.0
        
        # Random angle
        angle = np.random.random() * 2 * np.pi
        
        # Random distance (exponential distribution for privacy)
        distance = np.random.exponential(radius_deg / 2)
        
        # Calculate offset
        lat_offset = distance * np.cos(angle)
        lng_offset = distance * np.sin(angle) / np.cos(np.radians(lat))
        
        return (lat + lat_offset, lng + lng_offset)
4.2 Data Retention & Deletion
python
# data_retention.py
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import asyncio

class DataRetention:
    """
    Manages data retention policies and automatic deletion.
    """
    
    RETENTION_POLICIES = {
        'location_emergency': timedelta(days=30),
        'location_standard': timedelta(days=7),
        'audio_recordings': timedelta(days=90),
        'device_scans_raw': timedelta(hours=24),
        'device_scans_anonymized': timedelta(days=90),
        'alert_records': timedelta(days=365),
        'audit_logs': timedelta(days=365 * 7),  # 7 years
        'guardian_relationships': None,  # Keep until deleted by user
        'user_accounts': None,  # Keep until deleted
    }
    
    async def purge_expired_data(self):
        """Run daily purge of expired data."""
        for data_type, retention in self.RETENTION_POLICIES.items():
            if retention is None:
                continue
            
            cutoff = datetime.now() - retention
            
            if data_type == 'location_emergency':
                await self._purge_emergency_locations(cutoff)
            elif data_type == 'audio_recordings':
                await self._purge_audio_recordings(cutoff)
            elif data_type == 'device_scans_raw':
                await self._purge_raw_scans(cutoff)
            # ... etc
    
    async def delete_user_data(self, user_id: str):
        """
        Complete user data deletion (GDPR/NDPR right to erasure).
        """
        # Delete user data from all databases
        await self._delete_from_postgres(user_id)
        await self._delete_from_neo4j(user_id)
        await self._delete_from_redis(user_id)
        await self._delete_from_ipfs(user_id)
        await self._delete_from_blockchain(user_id)  # Mark as deleted, don't remove
        
        # Log deletion
        await self._log_deletion(user_id)

5.1 Intrusion Detection Rules
yaml
# ids_rules.yaml
rules:
  - name: "Excessive failed authentication"
    condition: "count(failed_auth) > 10 in 5 minutes"
    action: "block_ip_temporary"
    duration: "30 minutes"
    severity: "medium"
    
  - name: "PII access outside business hours"
    condition: "pii_access AND hour NOT BETWEEN 6 AND 22"
    action: "alert_security_team"
    severity: "high"
    
  - name: "Geographic anomaly"
    condition: "login_location_distance > 500km AND time_since_last_login < 1 hour"
    action: "require_mfa"
    severity: "high"
    
  - name: "Bulk alert export"
    condition: "export_count > 100 in 1 hour"
    action: "block_and_alert"
    severity: "critical"
    
  - name: "API key used from new IP"
    condition: "new_ip AND device_api_key"
    action: "verify_device"
    severity: "medium"
    
  - name: "Suspicious scan pattern"
    condition: "scan_frequency > 10x_normal AND not_emergency"
    action: "flag_device"
    severity: "low"
5.2 Incident Response Protocol
text
INCIDENT RESPONSE FLOWCHART:

[DETECT] → [CLASSIFY] → [CONTAIN] → [ERADICATE] → [RECOVER] → [LEARN]

1. DETECT (Automated)
   - IDS alert triggered
   - Anomaly detection flagged
   - User report received

2. CLASSIFY (Security Team - 15 minutes SLA)
   - Severity: Critical / High / Medium / Low
   - Scope: Single user / Region / System-wide
   - Type: Breach / Attempt / False alarm

3. CONTAIN (Immediate)
   - Critical: Isolate affected systems, rotate all keys
   - High: Block affected IPs, revoke compromised tokens
   - Medium: Increase monitoring, notify affected users
   - Low: Log for review

4. ERADICATE (24 hours SLA)
   - Identify root cause
   - Patch vulnerability
   - Remove attacker persistence

5. RECOVER (48 hours SLA)
   - Restore from clean backups
   - Verify data integrity
   - Reissue credentials

6. LEARN (1 week)
   - Post-mortem analysis
   - Update security controls
   - Update documentation
   - Share anonymized findings with community
End of Security Protocol Complete Documentation

```yaml
# terraform/gke-cluster.tf
resource "google_container_cluster" "aegis_production" {
  name     = "aegis-production"
  location = "europe-west2"
  
  # Multi-zone for high availability
  node_locations = [
    "europe-west2-a",
    "europe-west2-b",
    "europe-west2-c",
  ]
  
  # Enable GKE features
  enable_autopilot = false
  
  # Network policy for pod-to-pod security
  network_policy {
    enabled = true
    provider = "CALICO"
  }
  
  # Private cluster (nodes not directly accessible from internet)
  private_cluster_config {
    enable_private_nodes    = true
    enable_private_endpoint = false
    master_ipv4_cidr_block  = "172.16.0.0/28"
  }
  
  # IP aliasing for VPC-native networking
  ip_allocation_policy {
    cluster_secondary_range_name  = "pods"
    services_secondary_range_name = "services"
  }
  
  # Workload Identity for secure service-to-service auth
  workload_identity_config {
    workload_pool = "${var.project_id}.svc.id.goog"
  }
}

# Node pools for different workloads
resource "google_container_node_pool" "api_services" {

    max_node_count = 20
  }

      workload = "api"

# kubernetes/alert-service.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: alert-service
  namespace: aegis-production
  labels:
    app: alert-service
    component: core
spec:
  replicas: 5
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 2
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: alert-service
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: alert-service
        component: core
        version: "2.0.0"
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9090"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: alert-service-sa
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - labelSelector:
              matchExpressions:
              - key: app
                operator: In
                values:
                - alert-service
            topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      tolerations:
      - key: workload
        value: api
        effect: NoSchedule
      containers:
      - name: alert-service
        image: gcr.io/aegis-production/alert-service:2.0.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        - containerPort: 9090
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: RUST_LOG
          value: "info"
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: database-credentials
              key: url
        - name: REDIS_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: redis-credentials
              key: url
        - name: KAFKA_BROKERS
          value: "kafka-0.kafka:9092,kafka-1.kafka:9092,kafka-2.kafka:9092"
        resources:
          requests:
            cpu: "500m"
            memory: "512Mi"
          limits:
            cpu: "2000m"
            memory: "2Gi"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /healthz
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 3
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /startup
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 30

        periodSeconds: 60

  - "api.aegis.ng"

  - aegis-gateway

    route:
    - destination:
        host: alert-service
        port:
          number: 8080
      weight: 100
    retries:
      attempts: 3
      perTryTimeout: 5s
      retryOn: "5xx,reset,connect-failure"
    timeout: 15s
    
  - match:
    - uri:
        prefix: /v2/alerts
    route:
    - destination:
        host: alert-service
        port:
          number: 8080
    timeout: 10s
    
  - match:
    - uri:
        prefix: /v2/sentinel
    route:
    - destination:
        host: sentinel-service
        port:
          number: 8080
    timeout: 10s
    
  - match:
    - uri:
        prefix: /v2/risk
    route:
    - destination:
        host: risk-service
        port:
          number: 8080
    timeout: 5s
    
  # Public endpoints - rate limited
  - match:
    - uri:
        prefix: /v2/public
    route:
    - destination:
        host: public-service
        port:
          number: 8080
    timeout: 5s

3.0 CI/CD Pipeline
3.1 GitHub Actions Workflow
yaml
# .github/workflows/deploy-production.yml
name: Deploy to Production

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
    paths:
      - 'services/**'
      - 'libs/**'
      - '.github/workflows/**'
  workflow_dispatch:
    inputs:
      service:
        description: 'Service to deploy (all for everything)'
        required: false
        default: 'all'

env:
  GCP_PROJECT: aegis-production
  GCP_REGION: europe-west2
  GKE_CLUSTER: aegis-production

jobs:
  # =============================================
  # SECURITY SCAN
  # =============================================
  security-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Run Trivy vulnerability scanner
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          scan-type: 'fs'
          scan-ref: '.'
          format: 'sarif'
          output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
          severity: 'CRITICAL,HIGH'
      
      - name: Upload scan results
        uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3
        with:
          sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
      
      - name: Check for critical vulnerabilities
        run: |
          if grep -q "CRITICAL" trivy-results.sarif; then
            echo "CRITICAL vulnerabilities found! Blocking deployment."
            exit 1
          fi

  # =============================================
  # TEST
  # =============================================
  test:
    needs: security-scan
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [alert-service, sentinel-service, risk-service, guardian-service]
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Setup Rust
        uses: actions-rs/toolchain@v1
        with:
          toolchain: stable
      
      - name: Run unit tests
        working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
        run: cargo test --release
      
      - name: Run integration tests
        working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
        run: cargo test --release -- --ignored
        env:
          TEST_DATABASE_URL: ${{ secrets.TEST_DATABASE_URL }}
      
      - name: Generate code coverage
        run: |
          cargo tarpaulin --out Xml --output-dir coverage
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          files: coverage/cobertura.xml
          flags: ${{ matrix.service }}

  # =============================================
  # BUILD & PUSH
  # =============================================
  build:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push' || github.event.inputs.service == 'all' || github.event.inputs.service == matrix.service
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [alert-service, sentinel-service, risk-service, guardian-service, api-gateway]
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Authenticate to Google Cloud
        uses: google-github-actions/auth@v2
        with:
          credentials_json: '${{ secrets.GCP_SA_KEY }}'
      
      - name: Set up Cloud SDK
        uses: google-github-actions/setup-gcloud@v2
      
      - name: Configure Docker
        run: gcloud auth configure-docker gcr.io
      
      - name: Build Docker image
        run: |
          docker build \
            -t gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/${{ matrix.service }}:${{ github.sha }} \
            -t gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/${{ matrix.service }}:latest \
            -f services/${{ matrix.service }}/Dockerfile \
            .
      
      - name: Run container security scan
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          image-ref: gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/${{ matrix.service }}:${{ github.sha }}
          format: 'table'
          exit-code: '1'
          ignore-unfixed: true
          severity: 'CRITICAL'
      
      - name: Push Docker image
        run: |
          docker push gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/${{ matrix.service }}:${{ github.sha }}
          docker push gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/${{ matrix.service }}:latest

  # =============================================
  # DEPLOY
  # =============================================
  deploy:
    needs: build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Authenticate to Google Cloud
        uses: google-github-actions/auth@v2
        with:
          credentials_json: '${{ secrets.GCP_SA_KEY }}'
      
      - name: Get GKE credentials
        uses: google-github-actions/get-gke-credentials@v2
        with:
          cluster_name: ${{ env.GKE_CLUSTER }}
          location: ${{ env.GCP_REGION }}
      
      - name: Update Kubernetes deployments
        run: |
          # Update image tags for all services
          for service in alert-service sentinel-service risk-service guardian-service; do
            kubectl set image deployment/$service \
              $service=gcr.io/${{ env.GCP_PROJECT }}/$service:${{ github.sha }} \
              -n aegis-production
          done
      
      - name: Wait for rollout
        run: |
          for service in alert-service sentinel-service risk-service guardian-service; do
            kubectl rollout status deployment/$service -n aegis-production --timeout=300s
          done
      
      - name: Run smoke tests
        run: |
          # Test critical endpoints
          curl -f https://api.aegis.ng/healthz
          curl -f https://api.aegis.ng/v2/public/statistics
      
      - name: Notify on success
        if: success()
        uses: slackapi/slack-github-action@v1
        with:
          channel-id: 'deployments'
          slack-message: "✅ Production deployment successful! SHA: ${{ github.sha }}"
        env:
          SLACK_BOT_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SLACK_BOT_TOKEN }}
      
      - name: Notify on failure
        if: failure()
        uses: slackapi/slack-github-action@v1
        with:
          channel-id: 'alerts'
          slack-message: "🚨 Production deployment FAILED! SHA: ${{ github.sha }}. Rolling back..."
        env:
          SLACK_BOT_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SLACK_BOT_TOKEN }}
      - name: Rollback on failure
        if: failure()
        run: |
          for service in alert-service sentinel-service risk-service guardian-service; do
            kubectl rollout undo deployment/$service -n aegis-production
          done
4.0 Monitoring & Observability
4.1 Prometheus Configuration
yaml
# prometheus/alerts.yaml
groups:
  - name: aegis_critical
    rules:
      - alert: HighAlertLatency
        expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{endpoint="/v2/alerts/emergency"}[5m])) > 3
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          component: alert-service
        annotations:
          summary: "Alert endpoint P99 latency > 3 seconds"
          description: "Emergency alert endpoint is experiencing high latency. Current P99: {{ $value }}s"
      
      - alert: AlertProcessingBacklog
        expr: kafka_consumer_lag{topic="emergency-alerts"} > 100
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: critical
        annotations:
          summary: "Emergency alert processing backlog"
          description: "{{ $value }} alerts are queued and not yet processed"
      
      - alert: LoRaGatewayDown
        expr: absent(aegisnet_gateway_heartbeat) == 1
        for: 10m
        labels:
          severity: high
        annotations:
          summary: "LoRa gateway {{ $labels.gateway_id }} is offline"
          description: "Gateway has not sent heartbeat for 10 minutes"
      
      - alert: HighFalseAlarmRate
        expr: rate(alerts_cancelled_total[1h]) / rate(alerts_total[1h]) > 0.3
        for: 1h
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "High false alarm rate detected"
          description: "False alarm rate is {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}"
      
      - alert: DatabaseConnectionPoolExhaustion
        expr: db_connection_pool_active / db_connection_pool_max > 0.8
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: high
        annotations:
          summary: "Database connection pool near exhaustion"
          description: "{{ $value | humanizePercentage }} of connections in use"

5.0 Disaster Recovery
5.1 Backup Strategy
yaml
# terraform/backups.tf
resource "google_sql_database_instance" "aegis_postgres" {
  name             = "aegis-postgres"
  database_version = "POSTGRES_15"
  region           = "europe-west2"
  
  settings {
    tier = "db-custom-4-16384"
    
    backup_configuration {
      enabled                        = true
      start_time                     = "03:00"
      point_in_time_recovery_enabled = true
      transaction_log_retention_days = 7
      backup_retention_settings {
        retained_backups = 30
        retention_unit   = "COUNT"
      }
    }
    
    ip_configuration {
      ipv4_enabled    = false
      private_network = google_compute_network.aegis_vpc.id
    }
    
    # Automated daily backup to secondary region
    location_preference {
      zone                   = "europe-west2-a"
      secondary_zone         = "europe-west2-c"
    }
  }
}

# Cross-region backup for disaster recovery
resource "google_storage_bucket" "backups_bucket" {
  name          = "aegis-backups-eu"
  location      = "EU"
  storage_class = "STANDARD"
  
  versioning {
    enabled = true
  }
  
  lifecycle_rule {
    condition {
      age = 90
    }
    action {
      type = "Delete"
    }
  }
}
5.2 Recovery Runbook
markdown
# DISASTER RECOVERY RUNBOOK

## Scenario 1: Complete Cloud Provider Outage
1. Activate AWS failover region
2. Update DNS: api.aegis.ng → AWS load balancer
3. Promote read replicas to primary
4. Verify data consistency
5. Notify all users via SMS broadcast

## Scenario 2: Database Corruption
1. Stop write traffic to affected database
2. Initiate point-in-time recovery
3. Verify recovered data integrity
4. Resume traffic
5. Replay any lost transactions from Kafka

## Scenario 3: Security Breach
1. Isolate affected systems
2. Rotate all credentials
3. Restore from last known clean backup
4. Forensic analysis
5. Patch vulnerability
6. Gradual traffic restoration

## Recovery Time Objective (RTO): 1 hour
## Recovery Point Objective (RPO): 5 minutes (transaction log shipping)
End of DevOps Deployment Complete Documentation

## 2.0 Critical Test Scenarios

### 2.1 Emergency Alert Flow Tests

| ID | Scenario | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|----|----------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| E2E-001 | Full alert flow with GSM | User triggers alert → SMS sent → Guardians notified → Guardian acknowledges → Victim receives vibration | All steps complete < 10 seconds | P0 |
| E2E-002 | Alert flow without data | User triggers alert with airplane mode → SMS sent → HTTP queued → WiFi restored → HTTP delivered | Alert delivered via SMS only, HTTP retried | P0 |
| E2E-003 | Alert flow without GSM (LoRa) | User triggers alert → LoRa broadcast → Mesh relays → Gateway → MQTT → Alert Service | Alert delivered via mesh < 30 seconds | P0 |
| E2E-004 | Multiple simultaneous alerts | 50 users trigger alerts simultaneously | All processed, no data loss, response < 15 seconds | P0 |
| E2E-005 | Alert cancellation | User triggers → Cancels within 5 seconds | Guardians notified of cancellation | P1 |

### 2.2 Performance Tests

| ID | Scenario | Target | Tool |
|----|----------|--------|------|
| PERF-001 | Alert endpoint load test | 1000 requests/second, P99 < 1s | k6 |
| PERF-002 | Location update load | 10000 updates/second | k6 |
| PERF-003 | WebSocket connections | 50000 concurrent connections | Artillery |
| PERF-004 | Database query performance | Complex graph queries < 500ms | pgbench, Neo4j benchmarking |
| PERF-005 | SMS gateway throughput | 100 SMS/second | Africa's Talking sandbox |

### 2.3 Security Tests

| ID | Scenario | Tool | Frequency |
|----|----------|------|-----------|
| SEC-001 | Penetration testing | Burp Suite, OWASP ZAP | Quarterly |
| SEC-002 | Dependency scanning | Snyk, Dependabot | Continuous |
| SEC-003 | Secret scanning | GitGuardian, truffleHog | Pre-commit, CI |
| SEC-004 | Fuzzing | AFL, libFuzzer | Weekly |
| SEC-005 | Social engineering simulation | Custom | Biannually |
| SEC-006 | Physical security audit | On-site inspection | Quarterly |

# 14 - Regulatory Compliance Framework

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Jurisdiction:** Federal Republic of Nigeria
- **Primary Regulator:** NITDA

---

## 1.0 Legal Framework

### 1.1 Applicable Nigerian Laws

| Law | Relevance | Compliance Requirement |
|-----|-----------|----------------------|
| Nigeria Data Protection Regulation (NDPR) 2019 | Data privacy | Data Protection Impact Assessment, consent management |
| Cybercrimes Act 2015 | Computer systems | Lawful interception capability, evidence preservation |
| NCC Regulations | Telecommunications | Type approval for LoRa devices, frequency allocation |
| NITDA Guidelines | IT systems | Regulatory sandbox participation, security audits |
| Freedom of Information Act | Public data | Public portal transparency requirements |
| Administration of Criminal Justice Act | Evidence | Chain of custody for digital evidence |

### 1.2 Regulatory Sandbox Application

\`\`\`yaml
sandbox_application:
  applicant: "[Your Organization Name]"
  project_name: "Aegis Civilian Safety Grid"
  sandbox_duration: "12 months (renewable)"
  
  requested_exemptions:
    - "Limited frequency use for LoRa mesh (868 MHz ISM band)"
    - "Pilot deployment without full type approval (temporary)"

    - "NITDA Representative (Chair)"
    - "National Security Adviser Office Representative"
    - "Nigerian Communications Commission Representative"
    - "National Human Rights Commission Representative"
    - "Civil Society Organization Representative"
    - "[Your Organization] Chief Technical Officer"
    
  reporting_requirements:
    - "Monthly technical reports"
    - "Quarterly privacy audit reports"
    - "Incident reports within 24 hours"
    - "Biannual independent security audit"
\`\`\`

### 1.3 Data Protection Impact Assessment (DPIA)

**Data Categories Collected:**

| Category | Sensitivity | Legal Basis | Retention Period |
|----------|-------------|-------------|------------------|
| Location data (active alert) | High | Vital interests | 30 days (alert period) + 90 days (investigation) |
| Location data (Sentinel Mode) | Medium | Consent | 7 days (anonymized after 24 hours) |
| Audio recordings | High | Vital interests | 30 days (alert period) + 90 days (evidence) |
| Device MAC addresses (scanned) | Low | Legitimate interest | 24 hours (raw), 90 days (anonymized) |
| Phone numbers (guardians) | Medium | Consent | Until relationship removed |
| User identity | High | Contract | Duration of account + 2 years |

---

## 2.0 Privacy by Design Implementation

### 2.1 Data Minimization

\`\`\`python
# privacy_controller.py
class PrivacyController:
    """
    Implements privacy-by-design principles in all data operations.
    """
    
    @staticmethod
    def anonymize_location(lat: float, lng: float, precision: int = 3) -> tuple:
        """
        Reduce location precision for non-emergency data.
        precision=3 → ~100m accuracy
        precision=4 → ~10m accuracy (emergency only)
        """
        return (
            round(lat, precision),
            round(lng, precision)
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def hash_device_id(device_id: str) -> str:
        """One-way hash device identifiers for storage."""
        import hashlib
        return hashlib.sha256(
            device_id.encode() + SALT.encode()
        ).hexdigest()
    
    @staticmethod
    def apply_differential_privacy(data: list, epsilon: float = 0.1) -> list:
        """
        Add calibrated noise to protect individual privacy while 
        maintaining statistical validity.
        """
        import numpy as np
        sensitivity = 1.0
        noise_scale = sensitivity / epsilon
        noise = np.random.laplace(0, noise_scale, len(data))
        return [d + n for d, n in zip(data, noise)]
\`\`\`

---

## 3.0 Law Enforcement Access Protocol

### 3.1 Four-Eyes Principle

Access to identifiable data requires:
1. Valid court warrant
2. Two authorized system administrators (different organizations)
3. Hardware security key from each
4. Real-time logging to immutable audit trail
5. Notification to the subject (within 30 days, unless court orders delayed notification)

### 3.2 Emergency Access Exception

In active kidnapping situations, Command Center can access victim data without warrant. This access is:
- Logged immutably
- Reviewed within 24 hours by oversight committee
- Limited to active alert period

---

## 4.0 Oversight & Audit

### 4.1 Independent Audit Requirements

- **Quarterly:** NITDA-approved auditor reviews privacy controls
- **Biannually:** Independent penetration testing
- **Annually:** Full security audit with public summary report

### 4.2 Civil Society Oversight Board

- 5 members from recognized CSOs
- Real-time access to anonymized system metrics
- Monthly review of access logs
- Power to suspend operations if violations found

---

*End of Regulatory Compliance Document*



# 15 - Pilot Program Deployment Strategy

## Document Control
- **Version:** 2.0
- **Last Updated:** 2026-06-10
- **Target Region:** Kaduna State (Phase 1)

---

## 1.0 Pilot Overview

### 1.1 Objectives

1. Validate system functionality in real-world Nigerian conditions
2. Measure impact on kidnapping response times and outcomes
3. Gather user feedback for iteration
4. Build trust with communities and security forces
5. Generate data for regulatory approval

### 1.2 Success Metrics

| Metric | Baseline | Target | Measurement |
|--------|----------|--------|-------------|
| Alert-to-response time | 45+ minutes | < 15 minutes | System logs |
| Guardian acknowledgment rate | N/A | > 80% | System analytics |
| False alarm rate | N/A | < 15% | User surveys |
| Network uptime | N/A | > 99% | Monitoring |
| User retention (30-day) | N/A | > 60% | Analytics |
| Community trust score | N/A | > 7/10 | Surveys |

---

## 2.0 Pilot Phases

### Phase 0: Preparation (Month 1-2)
- [ ] Secure regulatory sandbox approval from NITDA
- [ ] Sign MOUs with Kaduna State Government, Police Command
- [ ] Recruit and vet pilot participants (500 users)
- [ ] Deploy 10 LoRa mesh nodes along Kaduna-Zaria corridor
- [ ] Train 20 police officers on Command Center
- [ ] Conduct community sensitization in 5 LGAs

### Phase 1: Alpha Testing (Month 3)
- 500 users (selected from high-risk communities)
- Limited to Sentinel App and SMS alerts
- No LoRa mesh (Phase 2)
- Daily monitoring and rapid bug fixes
- Weekly feedback sessions with user representatives

### Phase 2: Mesh Integration (Month 4-5)
- Activate LoRa mesh network
- Expand to 2,000 users
- Onboard 50 guardians
- Integrate with police response protocols
- Begin public portal (limited to pilot area)

### Phase 3: Full Pilot (Month 6-8)
- 5,000 users
- Full feature set including Journey Mode, Sentinel Mode
- 100 mesh nodes
- Command Center at Kaduna Police HQ
- Public portal with pilot area data
- Monthly impact assessments

### Phase 4: Evaluation & Expansion (Month 9-12)
- Independent academic evaluation
- Regulatory report to NITDA
- Decision on state-wide rollout
- Expansion planning to other high-risk states

---

## 3.0 Community Engagement

### 3.1 Trust Building Strategy
TRADITIONAL LEADERS FIRST

Brief Emirs, Chiefs, Village Heads

Obtain traditional endorsements

Use traditional communication channels

RELIGIOUS INSTITUTIONS

Brief Imams, Pastors

Friday sermon / Sunday service announcements

Faith-based trust networks

COMMUNITY MEETINGS

Town halls in each pilot LGA

Live demonstrations

Q&A sessions with technical team

PILOT CHAMPIONS

Recruit respected community members

Train them as first-line support

Incentivize with stipends

TRANSPARENCY

Public dashboard with pilot metrics

Regular community feedback reports

Independent oversight visible

text

### 3.2 Risk Mitigation

| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|------|------------|--------|------------|
| Kidnappers target pilot participants | Low | Critical | Anonymous participation, no public lists |
| System failure during emergency | Medium | Critical | SMS fallback, extensive testing |
| Community mistrust | Medium | High | Traditional leader endorsements, transparency |
| Police misuse of data | Low | High | Strict access controls, CSO oversight |
| False sense of security | Medium | Medium | Clear communication of limitations |

---

## 4.0 Training Program

### 4.1 User Training (Sentinel App)

**Format:** Community-based workshops (2 hours)
**Content:**
1. What Aegis is and is NOT
2. Installing and setting up the app
3. Adding guardians
4. Triggering an emergency (practice)
5. Sentinel Mode activation
6. Journey Mode for travel
7. Understanding vibration patterns
8. Privacy and data protection

**Materials:**
- Illustrated guide in Hausa, Yoruba, Igbo, Pidgin, English
- Video tutorial (offline, pre-loaded on devices)
- Quick reference card (waterproof)

### 4.2 Command Center Training (Police)

**Format:** 3-day intensive workshop
**Content:**
- Day 1: System overview, alert monitoring, map navigation
- Day 2: Alert response protocols, unit dispatching, escalation
- Day 3: Simulation exercises, intelligence analysis, reporting
